Safe Continual Reinforcement Learning in Non-stationary Environments
Authors: Austin Coursey, Abel Diaz-Gonzalez, Marcos Quinones-Grueiro, Gautam Biswas
First: 2026-04-21T17:58:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T17:58:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) offers a compelling data-driven paradigm for synthesizing controllers for complex systems when accurate physical models are unavailable; however, most existing control-oriented RL methods assume stationarity and, therefore, struggle in real-world non-stationary deployments where system dynamics and operating conditions can change unexpectedly. Moreover, RL controllers acting in physical environments must satisfy safety constraints throughout their learning and execution phases, rendering transient violations during adaptation unacceptable. Although continual RL and safe RL have each addressed non-stationarity and safety, respectively, their intersection remains comparatively unexplored, motivating the study of safe continual RL algorithms that can adapt over the system's lifetime while preserving safety. In this work, we systematically investigate safe continual reinforcement learning by introducing three benchmark environments that capture safety-critical continual adaptation and by evaluating representative approaches from safe RL, continual RL, and their combinations. Our empirical results reveal a fundamental tension between maintaining safety constraints and preventing catastrophic forgetting under non-stationary dynamics, with existing methods generally failing to achieve both objectives simultaneously. To address this shortcoming, we examine regularization-based strategies that partially mitigate this trade-off and characterize their benefits and limitations. Finally, we outline key open challenges and research directions toward developing safe, resilient learning-based controllers capable of sustained autonomous operation in changing environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非平稳环境下的安全持续强化学习
强化学习（RL）为缺乏精确物理模型的复杂系统提供了一种基于数据驱动的控制器合成范式；然而，现有大多数面向控制的RL方法假设环境是平稳的，因此在系统动态和运行条件可能意外变化的现实非平稳部署中表现不佳。此外，在物理环境中运行的RL控制器必须在学习和执行阶段始终满足安全约束，这使得适应过程中的临时违规不可接受。尽管持续RL和安全RL已分别针对非平稳性和安全性进行了研究，但二者的交叉领域仍相对未被探索，这推动了对安全持续RL算法的研究，使其能在系统生命周期中适应变化同时保持安全性。本文通过引入三个捕捉安全关键持续适应任务的基准环境，并评估来自安全RL、持续RL及其组合的代表性方法，系统性地研究了安全持续强化学习。实证结果揭示了在非平稳动态下维持安全约束与防止灾难性遗忘之间的根本矛盾，现有方法通常无法同时实现这两个目标。为弥补这一不足，我们研究了基于正则化的策略，这些策略部分缓解了上述权衡，并分析了其优势与局限。最后，我们概述了关键开放挑战与研究方向，以推动开发能够在变化环境中持续自主运行的安全、鲁棒的基于学习的控制器。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the need for reinforcement learning (RL) controllers to operate safely in real-world non-stationary environments, where system dynamics can change unexpectedly, and safety constraints must be upheld continuously without transient violations. The method involves systematically investigating safe continual RL by introducing three benchmark environments for safety-critical continual adaptation and evaluating representative approaches from safe RL, continual RL, and their combinations. The main experimental results reveal a fundamental tension between maintaining safety and preventing catastrophic forgetting under non-stationary dynamics, with existing methods generally failing to achieve both objectives simultaneously; regularization-based strategies are examined and shown to partially mitigate this trade-off, though limitations persist.
本研究的动机源于强化学习控制器需要在现实世界的非平稳环境中安全运行，其中系统动力学可能意外变化，且必须持续满足安全约束而不出现瞬时违规。方法上，通过引入三个用于安全关键持续适应的基准环境，并评估来自安全强化学习、持续强化学习及其组合的代表性方法，系统性地研究了安全持续强化学习。主要实验结果表明，在非平稳动态下，维持安全与防止灾难性遗忘之间存在根本性张力，现有方法通常无法同时实现这两个目标；研究检验了基于正则化的策略，发现其能部分缓解这一权衡，但仍存在局限性。
FASTER: Value-Guided Sampling for Fast RL
Authors: Perry Dong, Alexander Swerdlow, Dorsa Sadigh, Chelsea Finn
First: 2026-04-21T17:52:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T17:52:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Some of the most performant reinforcement learning algorithms today can be prohibitively expensive as they use test-time scaling methods such as sampling multiple action candidates and selecting the best one. In this work, we propose FASTER, a method for getting the benefits of sampling-based test-time scaling of diffusion-based policies without the computational cost by tracing the performance gain of action samples back to earlier in the denoising process. Our key insight is that we can model the denoising of multiple action candidates and selecting the best one as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) where the goal is to progressively filter action candidates before denoising is complete. With this MDP, we can learn a policy and value function in the denoising space that predicts the downstream value of action candidates in the denoising process and filters them while maximizing returns. The result is a method that is lightweight and can be plugged into existing generative RL algorithms. Across challenging long-horizon manipulation tasks in online and batch-online RL, FASTER consistently improves the underlying policies and achieves the best overall performance among the compared methods. Applied to a pretrained VLA, FASTER achieves the same performance while substantially reducing training and inference compute requirements. Code is available at https://github.com/alexanderswerdlow/faster .
中文标题/摘要
标题：FASTER：面向快速强化学习的价值引导采样方法
当前部分性能最优的强化学习算法因采用测试阶段扩展方法（如采样多个候选动作并择优执行）而计算成本极高。本研究提出FASTER方法，通过将动作样本的性能增益追溯至去噪过程早期阶段，在保持基于采样的扩散策略测试扩展优势的同时规避计算开销。核心思路在于：将多候选动作去噪择优过程建模为马尔可夫决策过程，其目标是在去噪完成前逐步筛选候选动作。基于该MDP框架，我们可在去噪空间学习策略与价值函数，用以预测候选动作在去噪流程中的下游价值，并在最大化回报的同时进行筛选。该方法具有轻量化特性，可嵌入现有生成式强化学习算法。在在线与批量在线强化学习的长期复杂操控任务中，FASTER持续提升基础策略性能，并在对比方法中取得最优综合表现。应用于预训练视觉语言模型时，FASTER在显著降低训练与推理计算需求的同时保持同等性能。代码已开源：https://github.com/alexanderswerdlow/faster。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for FASTER is to reduce the computational expense of sampling-based test-time scaling in reinforcement learning, which often involves generating multiple action candidates to select the best. The method reframes the denoising process of diffusion-based policies as a Markov Decision Process, enabling early filtering of action candidates by learning a value function that predicts downstream returns, thus allowing efficient pruning before denoising completes. Experimental results show that FASTER consistently improves policies in long-horizon manipulation tasks, achieving top performance in online and batch-online RL, and when applied to a pretrained VLA, it matches performance while significantly cutting training and inference compute costs.
FASTER的动机是降低强化学习中基于采样的测试时扩展的计算成本，该方法通常需要生成多个动作候选以选择最佳。该方法将基于扩散的策略的去噪过程重新构建为马尔可夫决策过程，通过学习预测下游回报的价值函数，在去噪完成前高效筛选动作候选。实验结果表明，在在线和批量在线强化学习的长期操作任务中，FASTER持续提升基础策略性能，并在对比方法中取得最佳整体表现；应用于预训练的VLA时，它在保持相同性能的同时大幅减少了训练和推理的计算需求。
Learning Hybrid-Control Policies for High-Precision In-Contact Manipulation Under Uncertainty
Authors: Hunter L. Brown, Geoffrey Hollinger, Stefan Lee
First: 2026-04-21T16:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T16:55:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning-based control policies have been frequently demonstrated to be more effective than analytical techniques for many manipulation tasks. Commonly, these methods learn neural control policies that predict end-effector pose changes directly from observed state information. For tasks like inserting delicate connectors which induce force constraints, pose-based policies have limited explicit control over force and rely on carefully tuned low-level controllers to avoid executing damaging actions. In this work, we present hybrid position-force control policies that learn to dynamically select when to use force or position control in each control dimension. To improve learning efficiency of these policies, we introduce Mode-Aware Training for Contact Handling (MATCH) which adjusts policy action probabilities to explicitly mirror the mode selection behavior in hybrid control. We validate MATCH's learned policy effectiveness using fragile peg-in-hole tasks under extreme localization uncertainty. We find MATCH substantially outperforms pose-control policies -- solving these tasks with up to 10% higher success rates and 5x fewer peg breaks than pose-only policies under common types of state estimation error. MATCH also demonstrates data efficiency equal to pose-control policies, despite learning in a larger and more complex action space. In over 1600 sim-to-real experiments, we find MATCH succeeds twice as often as pose policies in high noise settings (33% vs.~68%) and applies ~30% less force on average compared to variable impedance policies on a Franka FR3 in laboratory conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：不确定性条件下高精度接触式操作的混合控制策略学习
基于强化学习的控制策略在许多操作任务中已被证明比解析方法更有效。这类方法通常通过学习神经控制策略，直接从观测状态信息预测末端执行器的位姿变化。对于插入精密连接器等产生力约束的任务，基于位姿的策略对力的显式控制有限，需依赖精心调校的低层控制器以避免执行破坏性动作。本研究提出混合位置-力控制策略，能动态选择各控制维度何时采用力控或位姿控制。为提升策略学习效率，我们引入接触处理的模式感知训练方法，通过调整策略动作概率显式映射混合控制中的模式选择行为。在极端定位不确定性条件下，通过精密轴孔装配任务验证了该方法的策略有效性。实验表明：在常见状态估计误差类型下，该方法较纯位姿控制策略成功率提升最高达10%，零件破损减少5倍；尽管在更大更复杂的动作空间中学习，其数据效率与位姿控制策略相当。在超过1600次仿真到现实实验中，该方法在高噪声环境下的成功率是位姿策略的两倍（68%对33%），且在实验室条件下，相比Franka FR3机器人的可变阻抗策略平均施力减少约30%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of pose-based reinforcement learning policies in delicate manipulation tasks like connector insertion, where explicit force control is crucial to avoid damage, this paper introduces a hybrid position-force control policy that dynamically selects control modes per dimension. The method, enhanced by Mode-Aware Training for Contact Handling (MATCH), improves learning efficiency by aligning policy actions with hybrid control mode selection. Experimental results on fragile peg-in-hole tasks under localization uncertainty show that MATCH achieves up to 10% higher success rates and 5x fewer peg breaks compared to pose-only policies, with equal data efficiency and, in sim-to-real tests, doubles success rates in high-noise settings while applying 30% less force than variable impedance policies.
针对基于姿态的强化学习策略在精密操作任务（如连接器插入）中因缺乏显式力控制而易造成损坏的局限性，本文提出了一种混合位置-力控制策略，能动态选择各维度的控制模式。该方法通过模式感知接触处理训练（MATCH）提升学习效率，使策略行为与混合控制模式选择保持一致。在定位不确定性下的脆弱孔轴装配任务实验中，MATCH相比纯姿态策略实现了高达10%的成功率提升和5倍的轴断裂减少，且数据效率相当；在仿真到现实的测试中，高噪声环境下成功率翻倍，并在实验室条件下比可变阻抗策略平均减少约30%的施加力。
Fitted Q Evaluation Without Bellman Completeness via Stationary Weighting
Authors: Lars van der Laan, Nathan Kallus
First: 2025-12-29T19:04:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:40:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fitted Q-evaluation (FQE) is a foundational method for off-policy evaluation in reinforcement learning, but existing theory typically relies on Bellman completeness of the function class, a condition often violated in practice. This reliance is due to a fundamental norm mismatch: the Bellman operator is gamma-contractive in the L^2 norm induced by the target policy's stationary distribution, whereas standard FQE fits Bellman regressions under the behavior distribution. To resolve this mismatch, we reweight each Bellman regression step by an estimate of the stationary density ratio, inspired by emphatic weighting in temporal-difference learning. This makes the update behave as if it were performed under the target stationary distribution, restoring contraction without Bellman completeness while preserving the simplicity of regression-based evaluation. Illustrative experiments, including Baird's classical counterexample, show that stationary weighting can stabilize FQE under off-policy sampling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于平稳分布加权的免贝尔曼完备性拟合Q评估方法
拟合Q评估（FQE）是强化学习中离策略评估的基础方法，但现有理论通常依赖于函数类的贝尔曼完备性条件，该条件在实践中常不成立。这种依赖源于根本性的范数失配：贝尔曼算子在目标策略平稳分布诱导的L^2范数下具有γ收缩性，而标准FQE在行为分布下进行贝尔曼回归拟合。为解决此失配问题，我们受时序差分学习中强调加权思想的启发，通过平稳密度比估计对每个贝尔曼回归步骤进行重加权。这使得更新过程如同在目标平稳分布下执行，从而在不依赖贝尔曼完备性的条件下恢复收缩性，同时保持基于回归评估的简洁性。包括Baird经典反例在内的示例实验表明，平稳分布加权能稳定离策略采样下的FQE。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the reliance of fitted Q-evaluation (FQE) on Bellman completeness, a condition often not met in practice, which stems from a norm mismatch between the behavior distribution used in regression and the target policy's stationary distribution. The method introduces stationary weighting, which reweights each Bellman regression step with an estimate of the stationary density ratio, effectively aligning the update with the target distribution and restoring contraction without requiring Bellman completeness. Experimental results, including tests on Baird's counterexample, demonstrate that this approach stabilizes FQE under off-policy sampling, maintaining the simplicity of regression-based evaluation while overcoming previous limitations.
本研究的动机是解决拟合Q评估（FQE）对贝尔曼完备性的依赖问题，该条件在实践中常不满足，这源于回归中使用的行为分布与目标策略的平稳分布之间的范数不匹配。方法引入了平稳加权，通过估计平稳密度比对每个贝尔曼回归步骤进行重新加权，使更新与目标分布对齐，从而在不要求贝尔曼完备性的情况下恢复收缩性。实验结果包括在Baird经典反例上的测试表明，该方法能在离策略采样下稳定FQE，在保持基于回归的评估简洁性的同时克服了先前限制。
Reasoning Over Space: Enabling Geographic Reasoning for LLM-Based Generative Next POI Recommendation
Authors: Dongyi Lv, Qiuyu Ding, Heng-Da Xu, Zhaoxu Sun, Zhi Wang, Feng Xiong, Mu Xu
First: 2026-01-08T03:46:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:25:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative recommendation with large language models (LLMs) reframes prediction as sequence generation, yet existing LLM-based recommenders remain limited in leveraging geographic signals that are crucial in mobility and local-services scenarios. Here, we present Reasoning Over Space (ROS), a framework that utilizes geography as a vital decision variable within the reasoning process. ROS introduces a Hierarchical Spatial Semantic ID (SID) that discretizes coarse-to-fine locality and POI semantics into compositional tokens, and endows LLM with a three-stage Mobility Chain-of-Thought (CoT) paradigm that models user personality, constructs an intent-aligned candidate space, and performs locality informed pruning. We further align the model with real world geography via spatial-guided Reinforcement Learning (RL). Experiments on three widely used location-based social network (LBSN) datasets show that ROS achieves over 10% relative gains in hit rate over strongest LLM-based baselines and improves cross-city transfer, despite using a smaller backbone model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：空间推理：为基于大语言模型的生成式下一兴趣点推荐赋予地理推理能力
基于大语言模型（LLMs）的生成式推荐将预测重构为序列生成，但现有基于LLM的推荐系统在利用地理信号方面仍存在局限，而地理信号在移动性和本地服务场景中至关重要。本文提出“空间推理”（ROS）框架，将地理信息作为推理过程中的关键决策变量。ROS引入分层空间语义ID（SID），将粗粒度到细粒度的地理位置与兴趣点语义离散化为组合标记，并通过三阶段移动思维链（CoT）范式赋予LLM能力：建模用户特征、构建意图对齐的候选空间、执行基于地理信息的剪枝。我们进一步通过空间引导的强化学习（RL）使模型与现实世界地理对齐。在三个广泛使用的基于位置的社交网络（LBSN）数据集上的实验表明，即使使用更小的骨干模型，ROS在命中率上仍比最强的基于LLM的基线获得超过10%的相对提升，并改善了跨城市迁移性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limited use of geographic signals in existing large language model (LLM)-based generative recommenders for mobility and local services, this paper introduces the Reasoning Over Space (ROS) framework to incorporate geography as a key reasoning variable. The method employs a Hierarchical Spatial Semantic ID to tokenize location and point-of-interest (POI) semantics, coupled with a three-stage Mobility Chain-of-Thought paradigm that models user traits, builds an intent-aligned candidate set, and performs locality-aware pruning, further refined via spatial-guided reinforcement learning. Experimental results on three location-based social network datasets demonstrate that ROS achieves over 10% relative improvement in hit rate compared to leading LLM-based baselines and enhances cross-city transferability, even with a smaller backbone model.
针对现有基于大语言模型（LLM）的生成式推荐在移动性和本地服务场景中难以有效利用关键地理信号的问题，本文提出了空间推理（ROS）框架，将地理信息作为推理过程中的核心决策变量。该方法采用分层空间语义ID对粗粒度到细粒度的位置及兴趣点（POI）语义进行组合式标记，并结合三阶段移动思维链范式，建模用户个性、构建意图对齐的候选集并进行局部感知剪枝，进一步通过空间引导的强化学习实现与真实地理的对齐。在三个广泛使用的位置社交网络数据集上的实验表明，ROS相比最强的LLM基线在命中率上取得了超过10%的相对提升，并改善了跨城市迁移能力，尽管使用了更小的骨干模型。
Lyapunov-Certified Direct Switching Theory for Q-Learning
Authors: Donghwan Lee
First: 2026-04-21T15:22:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:22:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Q-learning is one of the most fundamental algorithms in reinforcement learning. We analyze constant-stepsize Q-learning through a direct stochastic switching system representation. The key observation is that the Bellman maximization error can be represented exactly by a stochastic policy. Therefore, the Q-learning error admits a switched linear conditional-mean recursion with martingale-difference noise. The intrinsic drift rate is the joint spectral radius (JSR) of the direct switching family, which can be strictly smaller than the standard row-sum rate. Using this representation, we derive a finite-time final-iterate bound via a JSR-induced Lyapunov function and then give a computable quadratic-certificate version.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Q学习的李雅普诺夫认证直接切换理论
Q学习是强化学习中最基础的算法之一。我们通过直接随机切换系统表示法分析恒定步长的Q学习。关键发现是贝尔曼最大化误差可精确表示为随机策略。因此，Q学习误差具有带鞅差噪声的切换线性条件均值递归特性。其内在漂移率为直接切换族的联合谱半径，该值可能严格小于标准行和速率。基于此表示，我们通过JSR诱导的李雅普诺夫函数推导出有限时间最终迭代界，进而给出可计算的二次认证版本。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for a more precise finite-time analysis of constant-stepsize Q-learning, this paper introduces a direct stochastic switching system representation that exactly captures the Bellman maximization error as a stochastic policy. The method leverages this representation to show that the Q-learning error follows a switched linear recursion with martingale-difference noise, where the intrinsic drift is governed by the joint spectral radius (JSR) of a switching family, potentially tighter than standard bounds. The main experimental results include the derivation of a finite-time final-iterate error bound using a JSR-induced Lyapunov function and the provision of a computable quadratic-certificate version, offering a novel analytical framework for certification.
本文旨在对恒定步长Q学习进行更精确的有限时间分析，其动机源于现有理论的局限。方法上，论文提出了一种直接随机切换系统表示，将贝尔曼最大化误差精确表示为随机策略，从而将Q学习误差建模为具有鞅差噪声的切换线性递归，其内在漂移率由切换族的联合谱半径（JSR）决定，该指标可能比标准行和率更严格。主要实验结果包括：利用JSR诱导的Lyapunov函数推导出有限时间最终迭代误差界，并给出了一个可计算的二次证书版本，为强化学习算法的认证提供了新的分析框架。
Multi-modal Reasoning with LLMs for Visual Semantic Arithmetic
Authors: Chuou Xu, Liya Ji, Qifeng Chen
First: 2026-04-21T15:19:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:19:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) as post-training is crucial for enhancing the reasoning ability of large language models (LLMs) in coding and math. However, their capacity for visual semantic arithmetic, inferring relationships from images, remains underexplored. The classic text analogy "king"-"man"+"woman" = "queen" illustrates relational reasoning, yet replacing text with images of "king" and "man" significantly reduces performance because it requires commonsense knowledge and the extraction of concise concepts from irrelevant visual details. This capability is important for service and domestic robotics in unstructured environments, where robots must infer semantic relationships among objects, agents, and actions. In a kitchen, recognizing from images that "powder" and "cake" are related by "is made of" grounds symbolic relations in perception, enabling tool substitution, task generalization, and improved semantic reasoning. Prior work approaches semantic arithmetic by decoding image features after vector arithmetic, but suffers from modality gaps and lacks systematic evaluation. In this paper, we formulate two novel tasks, two-term subtraction and three-term operations, and construct the Image-Relation-Pair Dataset (IRPD) for benchmarking. We further propose Semantic Arithmetic Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (SAri-RFT), which post-trains large vision-language models (LVLMs) using a verifiable function and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Our method achieves state-of-the-art results on IRPD and the real-world Visual7W-Telling dataset. By equipping LVLMs with robust cross-modal relational reasoning, this work advances domestic robots' ability to ground symbolic reasoning in perception, enhancing decision-making, tool adaptability, and human-robot interaction in complex environments. Datasets and source code are provided in the supplementary material.

标题：基于大语言模型的多模态视觉语义算术推理
强化学习作为后训练方法对提升大语言模型在编程与数学领域的推理能力至关重要，但其通过图像推断语义关系的视觉语义算术能力尚未得到充分探索。经典文本类比“国王”-“男人”+“女人”=“女王”展示了关系推理，但将文本替换为“国王”和“男人”的图像会显著降低性能，因为这需要常识知识并从无关视觉细节中提取核心概念。该能力对非结构化环境中的服务和家用机器人尤为重要，机器人需推断物体、智能体与动作间的语义关系。例如在厨房场景中，通过图像识别“粉末”与“蛋糕”存在“由...制成”的关系，能将符号关系锚定于感知中，从而支持工具替换、任务泛化和语义推理提升。现有研究通过向量运算后解码图像特征实现语义算术，但存在模态鸿沟且缺乏系统评估。本文提出两项新任务（二项减法和三项运算），构建了用于基准测试的图像关系对数据集（IRPD），并进一步提出语义算术强化微调方法（SAri-RFT），该方法通过可验证函数和组相对策略优化对大型视觉语言模型进行后训练。我们的方法在IRPD和真实世界Visual7W-Telling数据集上取得了最优结果。通过赋予大型视觉语言模型鲁棒的跨模态关系推理能力，本研究提升了家用机器人在感知中锚定符号推理的能力，增强了复杂环境下的决策制定、工具适应性和人机交互。数据集与源代码详见补充材料。

ASVSim (AirSim for Surface Vehicles): A High-Fidelity Simulation Framework for Autonomous Surface Vehicle Research
Authors: Bavo Lesy, Siemen Herremans, Robin Kerstens, Jan Steckel, Walter Daems, Siegfried Mercelis, Ali Anwar
First: 2025-06-27T12:39:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T15:14:46+00:00
Comments: 18 Pages, 13 Figures. Accepted at IEEE ACCESS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The transport industry has recently shown significant interest in unmanned surface vehicles (USVs), specifically for port and inland waterway transport. These systems can improve operational efficiency and safety, which is especially relevant in the European Union, where initiatives such as the Green Deal are driving a shift towards increased use of inland waterways. At the same time, a shortage of qualified personnel is accelerating the adoption of autonomous solutions. However, there is a notable lack of open-source, high-fidelity simulation frameworks and datasets for developing and evaluating such solutions. To address these challenges, we introduce AirSim for Surface Vehicles (ASVSim), an open-source simulation framework specifically designed for autonomous shipping research in inland and port environments. The framework combines simulated vessel dynamics with marine sensor simulation capabilities, including radar and camera systems and supports the generation of synthetic datasets for training computer vision models and reinforcement learning (RL) agents. Built upon Cosys-AirSim, ASVSim provides a comprehensive platform for developing autonomous navigation algorithms and generating synthetic datasets. The simulator supports research of both traditional control methods and deep learning-based approaches. Through experiments in waterway segmentation and autonomous navigation, we demonstrate the capabilities of the simulator in these research areas. ASVSim is provided as an open-source project under the MIT license, making autonomous navigation research accessible to a larger part of the ocean engineering community. See https://github.com/BavoLesy/ASVSim.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ASVSim（水面载具版AirSim）：面向自主水面载具研究的高保真仿真框架
近年来，交通运输行业对无人水面载具（USV）展现出浓厚兴趣，尤其在港口与内河运输领域。这类系统能提升运营效率与安全性，在欧盟地区尤为关键——《绿色协议》等倡议正推动内河航运的扩大应用。与此同时，专业人员短缺正加速自主解决方案的采用。然而，当前明显缺乏用于开发与评估此类方案的开源高保真仿真框架及数据集。为应对这些挑战，我们推出水面载具版AirSim（ASVSim）——专为内河及港口环境自主航运研究设计的开源仿真框架。该框架融合船舶动力学仿真与海事传感器（含雷达与摄像系统）模拟功能，支持生成用于训练计算机视觉模型与强化学习智能体的合成数据集。基于Cosys-AirSim构建的ASVSim为开发自主导航算法与生成合成数据提供了完整平台，既支持传统控制方法研究，也兼容深度学习方案。通过水道分割与自主导航实验，我们验证了该仿真器在相关研究领域的应用潜力。ASVSim以MIT许可证开源发布，旨在推动更广泛海洋工程社群开展自主导航研究。详见：https://github.com/BavoLesy/ASVSim。

Cyber Defense Benchmark: Agentic Threat Hunting Evaluation for LLMs in SecOps
Authors: Alankrit Chona, Igor Kozlov, Ambuj Kumar
First: 2026-04-21T14:53:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T14:53:23+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 3 figures, 5 tables. Complete benchmark and hunt traces available on request
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce the Cyber Defense Benchmark, a benchmark for measuring how well large language model (LLM) agents perform the core SOC analyst task of threat hunting: given a database of raw Windows event logs with no guided questions or hints, identify the exact timestamps of malicious events. The benchmark wraps 106 real attack procedures from the OTRF Security-Datasets corpus - spanning 86 MITRE ATT&CK sub-techniques across 12 tactics - into a Gymnasium reinforcement-learning environment. Each episode presents the agent with an in-memory SQLite database of 75,000-135,000 log records produced by a deterministic campaign simulator that time-shifts and entity-obfuscates the raw recordings. The agent must iteratively submit SQL queries to discover malicious event timestamps and explicitly flag them, scored CTF-style against Sigma-rule-derived ground truth. Evaluating five frontier models - Claude Opus 4.6, GPT-5, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Kimi K2.5, and Gemini 3 Flash - on 26 campaigns covering 105 of 106 procedures, we find that all models fail dramatically: the best model (Claude Opus 4.6) submits correct flags for only 3.8% of malicious events on average, and no run across any model ever finds all flags. We define a passing score as >= 50% recall on every ATT&CK tactic - the minimum bar for unsupervised SOC deployment. No model passes: the leader clears this bar on 5 of 13 tactics and the remaining four on zero. These results suggest that current LLMs are poorly suited for open-ended, evidence-driven threat hunting despite strong performance on curated Q&A security benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：网络防御基准：面向安全运维中大型语言模型的智能威胁狩猎评估
我们提出网络防御基准，用于评估大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在执行安全运营中心（SOC）分析师核心任务——威胁狩猎时的表现：在无引导问题或提示的情况下，基于原始Windows事件日志数据库，精准定位恶意事件的时间戳。该基准将OTRF Security-Datasets语料库中106个真实攻击流程（涵盖12种战术下的86项MITRE ATT&CK子技术）封装为Gymnasium强化学习环境。每个训练周期向智能体提供一个包含7.5万至13.5万条日志记录的内存SQLite数据库，这些记录由确定性攻击模拟器生成，并对原始数据进行了时间偏移和实体混淆处理。智能体需通过迭代提交SQL查询来发现恶意事件时间戳并显式标记，采用基于Sigma规则生成的真实标签进行CTF式评分。通过对Claude Opus 4.6、GPT-5、Gemini 3.1 Pro、Kimi K2.5和Gemini 3 Flash五种前沿模型在涵盖106个流程中105个的26次攻击活动中的评估，我们发现所有模型均表现严重不足：最佳模型（Claude Opus 4.6）平均仅能正确标记3.8%的恶意事件，且所有模型均未实现全标记发现。我们将合格标准定义为在每个ATT&CK战术上达到≥50%召回率——这是无监督SOC部署的最低门槛。无一模型达标：领先模型仅在13个战术中的5个达到门槛，其余四个模型零达标。这些结果表明，尽管当前LLM在精心设计的问答式安全基准测试中表现优异，但其在开放式、证据驱动的威胁狩猎任务中适应性严重不足。

Motivated by the need to evaluate large language models (LLMs) for real-world, open-ended security operations tasks, this paper introduces the Cyber Defense Benchmark, which measures LLM agents' ability to perform threat hunting by identifying malicious event timestamps from raw Windows event logs without guided questions. BAPO: Boundary-Aware Policy Optimization for Reliable Agentic Search
Authors: Shiyu Liu, Yongjing Yin, Jianhao Yan, Yunbo Tang, Qinggang Zhang, Bei Li, Xin Chen, Jingang Wang, Xunliang Cai, Jinsong Su
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-16T07:06:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T14:08:51+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Conference. Code is available at https://github.com/Liushiyu-0709/BAPO-Reliable-Search
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
RL-based agentic search enables LLMs to solve complex questions via dynamic planning and external search. While this approach significantly enhances accuracy with agent policies optimized via large-scale reinforcement learning, we identify a critical gap in reliability: these agents fail to recognize their reasoning boundaries and rarely admit ``I DON'T KNOW'' (IDK) even when evidence is insufficient or reasoning reaches its limit. The lack of reliability often leads to plausible but unreliable answers, introducing significant risks in many real-world scenarios. To this end, we propose Boundary-Aware Policy Optimization (BAPO), a novel RL framework designed to cultivate reliable boundary awareness without compromising accuracy. BAPO introduces two key components: (i) a group-based boundary-aware reward that encourages an IDK response only when the reasoning reaches its limit, and (ii) an adaptive reward modulator that strategically suspends this reward during early exploration, preventing the model from exploiting IDK as a shortcut. Extensive experiments on four benchmarks demonstrate that BAPO substantially enhances the overall reliability of agentic search.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BAPO：面向可靠智能搜索的边界感知策略优化
基于强化学习的智能搜索使大语言模型能够通过动态规划和外部搜索解决复杂问题。尽管通过大规模强化学习优化的智能体策略显著提升了准确性，但我们发现其可靠性存在关键缺陷：这些智能体无法识别自身推理边界，即使在证据不足或推理达到极限时也极少承认“我不知道”（IDK）。可靠性的缺失常导致看似合理但不可靠的答案，在现实场景中带来重大风险。为此，我们提出边界感知策略优化（BAPO），这是一种在不牺牲准确性的前提下培养可靠边界感知能力的新型强化学习框架。BAPO包含两个核心组件：（1）基于分组的边界感知奖励机制，仅在推理达到极限时鼓励IDK响应；（2）自适应奖励调节器，在早期探索阶段策略性地暂停该奖励，防止模型将IDK作为捷径利用。在四个基准测试上的大量实验表明，BAPO显著提升了智能搜索的整体可靠性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a reliability gap in RL-based agentic search, where large language models (LLMs) often fail to admit uncertainty (e.g., saying "I DON'T KNOW") when evidence is insufficient, leading to plausible but unreliable answers. To tackle this, the authors propose Boundary-Aware Policy Optimization (BAPO), a reinforcement learning framework that incorporates a group-based boundary-aware reward to encourage IDK responses only at reasoning limits, along with an adaptive reward modulator to prevent shortcut exploitation during early training. Experimental results on four benchmarks show that BAPO significantly improves the overall reliability of agentic search without compromising accuracy.
本文针对基于强化学习的智能搜索中存在的可靠性问题，即大语言模型在证据不足或推理达到极限时很少承认不确定性（如回答“我不知道”），从而产生看似合理但不可靠的答案。为解决这一问题，作者提出了边界感知策略优化（BAPO），这是一个强化学习框架，通过引入基于群体的边界感知奖励来鼓励仅在推理极限时做出“我不知道”的响应，并采用自适应奖励调节器在早期探索中策略性地暂停该奖励，防止模型将其作为捷径。在四个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，BAPO在不牺牲准确性的前提下，显著提升了智能搜索的整体可靠性。
EVPO: Explained Variance Policy Optimization for Adaptive Critic Utilization in LLM Post-Training
Authors: Chengjun Pan, Shichun Liu, Jiahang Lin, Dingwei Zhu, Jiazheng Zhang, Shihan Dou, Songyang Gao, Zhenhua Han, Binghai Wang, Rui Zheng, Xuanjing Huang, Tao Gui, Yansong Feng
First: 2026-04-21T14:07:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T14:07:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) for LLM post-training faces a fundamental design choice: whether to use a learned critic as a baseline for policy optimization. Classical theory favors critic-based methods such as PPO for variance reduction, yet critic-free alternatives like GRPO have gained widespread adoption due to their simplicity and competitive performance. We show that in sparse-reward settings, a learned critic can inject estimation noise that exceeds the state signal it captures, increasing rather than reducing advantage variance. By casting baseline selection as a Kalman filtering problem, we unify PPO and GRPO as two extremes of the Kalman gain and prove that explained variance (EV), computable from a single training batch, identifies the exact boundary: positive EV indicates the critic reduces variance, while zero or negative EV signals that it inflates variance. Building on this insight, we propose Explained Variance Policy Optimization (EVPO), which monitors batch-level EV at each training step and adaptively switches between critic-based and batch-mean advantage estimation, provably achieving no greater variance than the better of the two at every step. Across four tasks spanning classical control, agentic interaction, and mathematical reasoning, EVPO consistently outperforms both PPO and GRPO regardless of which fixed baseline is stronger on a given task. Further analysis confirms that the adaptive gating tracks critic maturation over training and that the theoretically derived zero threshold is empirically optimal.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EVPO：基于解释方差的策略优化方法及其在大语言模型后训练中的自适应评判器应用
大语言模型后训练的强化学习面临核心设计选择：是否使用学习型评判器作为策略优化的基线。经典理论支持基于评判器的方法（如PPO）以降低方差，但无评判器方法（如GRPO）因简洁性和竞争力而广泛应用。研究表明，在稀疏奖励场景中，学习型评判器可能引入超出其捕获状态信号的估计噪声，反而增加优势方差。通过将基线选择建模为卡尔曼滤波问题，我们将PPO和GRPO统一为卡尔曼增益的两个极端，并证明解释方差（EV）——可通过单次训练批次计算——能精确界定边界：正EV表明评判器降低方差，零或负EV则意味着其扩大方差。基于此，我们提出解释方差策略优化方法（EVPO），该方法在每步训练中监控批次级EV，自适应切换基于评判器与批次均值优势估计的方式，理论上确保每一步的方差不超过两者中的较优者。在涵盖经典控制、智能体交互和数学推理的四类任务中，无论固定基线在特定任务上表现如何，EVPO均持续优于PPO和GRPO。进一步分析证实，自适应门控机制能追踪评判器在训练中的成熟度，且理论推导的零阈值具有实证最优性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the dilemma in reinforcement learning for LLM post-training of whether to use a learned critic for policy optimization, noting that while classical theory supports critic-based methods like PPO for variance reduction, critic-free approaches such as GRPO are popular due to simplicity. The authors demonstrate that in sparse-reward settings, a critic can introduce estimation noise that outweighs its benefits, increasing advantage variance. By framing baseline selection as a Kalman filtering problem, they unify PPO and GRPO as extremes of the Kalman gain and prove that explained variance (EV), computed from a single batch, determines when a critic reduces or inflates variance. They propose Explained Variance Policy Optimization (EVPO), which adaptively switches between critic-based and batch-mean advantage estimation based on batch-level EV, ensuring no greater variance than the better method at each step. Experiments across four tasks in control, agentic interaction, and mathematical reasoning show EVPO consistently outperforms both PPO and GRPO, with analysis confirming that adaptive gating tracks critic maturation and the zero EV threshold is empirically optimal.
本文针对大语言模型后训练中强化学习的一个基本设计选择——是否使用学习到的评论家进行策略优化——展开研究，指出尽管经典理论支持像PPO这样的基于评论家的方法以降低方差，但无评论家方法如GRPO因简单性和竞争性能而广泛采用。作者证明，在稀疏奖励设置中，评论家可能引入超过其捕获状态信号的估计噪声，从而增加而非减少优势方差。通过将基线选择建模为卡尔曼滤波问题，他们将PPO和GRPO统一为卡尔曼增益的两个极端，并证明从单个训练批次计算的可解释方差（EV）能精确界定边界：正EV表示评论家降低方差，而零或负EV表示其增加方差。基于此，他们提出可解释方差策略优化（EVPO），在每一步监控批次级EV，自适应地在基于评论家和批次平均优势估计之间切换，理论上确保方差不超过两者中更优者。在涵盖经典控制、智能体交互和数学推理的四个任务中，EVPO始终优于PPO和GRPO，无论固定基线在特定任务上哪个更强；进一步分析证实自适应门控能跟踪评论家在训练中的成熟度，且理论推导的零阈值在经验上是最优的。
Global Optimization of Gaussian Process Acquisition Functions Using a Piecewise-Linear Kernel Approximation
Authors: Yilin Xie, Shiqiang Zhang, Joel A. Paulson, Calvin Tsay
First: 2024-10-22T10:56:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T13:45:21+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 4 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization relies on iteratively constructing and optimizing an acquisition function. The latter turns out to be a challenging, non-convex optimization problem itself. Despite the relative importance of this step, most algorithms employ sampling- or gradient-based methods, which do not provably converge to global optima. This work investigates mixed-integer programming (MIP) as a paradigm for global acquisition function optimization. Specifically, our Piecewise-linear Kernel Mixed Integer Quadratic Programming (PK-MIQP) formulation introduces a piecewise-linear approximation for Gaussian process kernels and admits a corresponding MIQP representation for acquisition functions. The proposed method is applicable to uncertainty-based acquisition functions for any stationary or dot-product kernel. We analyze the theoretical regret bounds of the proposed approximation, and empirically demonstrate the framework on synthetic functions, constrained benchmarks, and a hyperparameter tuning task.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于分段线性核近似的高斯过程采集函数全局优化方法
贝叶斯优化依赖于迭代构建并优化采集函数，而后者本身是一个具有挑战性的非凸优化问题。尽管该步骤相对重要，多数算法仍采用基于采样或梯度的方法，这些方法无法保证收敛至全局最优解。本研究探讨了将混合整数规划作为全局采集函数优化的范式。具体而言，我们提出的分段线性核混合整数二次规划（PK-MIQP）公式引入了高斯过程核函数的分段线性近似，并为采集函数构建了相应的MIQP表示。该方法适用于任何平稳核或点积核的基于不确定性的采集函数。我们分析了所提近似的理论遗憾界，并通过合成函数、约束基准测试和超参数调优任务进行了实证验证。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of globally optimizing acquisition functions in Bayesian optimization, which are typically non-convex and often solved with methods lacking global convergence guarantees. The proposed method, PK-MIQP, formulates the optimization as a mixed-integer quadratic program by introducing a piecewise-linear approximation for Gaussian process kernels, enabling provable global optimization for uncertainty-based acquisition functions with stationary or dot-product kernels. Experimental results on synthetic functions, constrained benchmarks, and a hyperparameter tuning task empirically validate the framework's effectiveness, supported by an analysis of its theoretical regret bounds.
本文针对贝叶斯优化中采集函数全局优化的挑战，这类函数通常是非凸的，且常用方法缺乏全局收敛保证。所提出的PK-MIQP方法通过引入高斯过程核函数的分段线性近似，将优化问题表述为混合整数二次规划，从而为基于不确定性的采集函数（适用于平稳或点积核）提供了可证明的全局优化方案。在合成函数、约束基准测试和超参数调优任务上的实验结果实证了该框架的有效性，并辅以其理论遗憾界的分析。
Learning Evolution via Optimization Knowledge Adaptation
Authors: Chao Wang, Lingling Li, Licheng Jiao, Jiaxuan Zhao, Fang Liu, Shuyuan Yang
First: 2025-01-04T05:35:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T12:31:45+00:00
Comments: This work has been accepted by IEEE Transactions on Pattern Analysis and Machine Intelligence
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The iterative search process of evolutionary algorithms (EAs) encapsulates optimization knowledge within historical populations and fitness evaluations. Effective utilization of this knowledge is crucial for facilitating knowledge transfer and online adaptation. However, current research typically addresses these goals in isolation and faces distinct limitations: evolutionary sequential transfer optimization often suffers from incomplete utilization of prior knowledge, while adaptive strategies, utilizing real-time knowledge, are limited to tailoring specific evolutionary operators. To simultaneously achieve these two capabilities, we introduce the Optimization Knowledge Adaptation Evolutionary Model (OKAEM), a unified learnable evolutionary framework capable of adaptively updating parameters based on available optimization knowledge. By parameterizing evolutionary operators via attention mechanisms, OKAEM enables learnable update rules that facilitate the utilization of optimization knowledge via two phases: pre-training to integrate extensive prior knowledge for efficient transfer, and adaptive optimization to dynamically update parameters based on real-time knowledge. Experimental results confirm that OKAEM significantly outperforms state-of-the-art sequential transfer methods across 12 transfer scenarios via pre-training, and surpasses advanced learnable EAs solely through its self-tuning mechanism in prior-free settings. Beyond demonstrating practical utility in prompt tuning for vision-language models, ablation studies validate the necessity of the learnable components, while visualization analyses reveal the model's capacity to autonomously discover interpretable evolutionary principles. The code can be accessed at https://gitee.com/Anonymity_Paper/code-of-okaem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过优化知识适应实现进化学习
进化算法（EAs）的迭代搜索过程将优化知识封装在历史种群和适应度评估中。有效利用这些知识对于促进知识迁移和在线适应至关重要。然而，当前研究通常孤立地处理这些目标，并面临明显局限：进化序列迁移优化常因先验知识利用不充分而受限，而利用实时知识的自适应策略则仅限于调整特定进化算子。为同时实现这两种能力，本文提出了优化知识适应进化模型（OKAEM），这是一个统一的可学习进化框架，能够基于可用优化知识自适应更新参数。通过注意力机制参数化进化算子，OKAEM实现了可学习的更新规则，通过两个阶段促进优化知识的利用：预训练阶段整合广泛先验知识以实现高效迁移，自适应优化阶段基于实时知识动态更新参数。实验结果表明，OKAEM在12个迁移场景中通过预训练显著优于最先进的序列迁移方法，并在无先验设置中仅通过自调优机制超越先进可学习进化算法。除了在视觉语言模型的提示调优中展示实际效用外，消融研究验证了可学习组件的必要性，可视化分析则揭示了模型自主发现可解释进化原理的能力。代码可通过 https://gitee.com/Anonymity_Paper/code-of-okaem 访问。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to more fully leverage the optimization knowledge embedded in the evolutionary search process, addressing the limitations of existing methods that treat knowledge transfer and online adaptation separately. The authors propose the Optimization Knowledge Adaptation Evolutionary Model (OKAEM), a unified framework that parameterizes evolutionary operators using attention mechanisms to create learnable update rules, enabling both pre-training on prior knowledge for transfer and adaptive optimization using real-time knowledge. Experimental results demonstrate that OKAEM outperforms state-of-the-art sequential transfer methods across 12 scenarios and surpasses advanced learnable evolutionary algorithms in prior-free settings through self-tuning, with additional validation showing its practical utility in prompt tuning and its ability to discover interpretable evolutionary principles.

HP-Edit: A Human-Preference Post-Training Framework for Image Editing
Authors: Fan Li, Chonghuinan Wang, Lina Lei, Yuping Qiu, Jiaqi Xu, Jiaxiu Jiang, Xinran Qin, Zhikai Chen, Fenglong Song, Zhixin Wang, Renjing Pei, Wangmeng Zuo
First: 2026-04-21T12:29:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T12:29:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Common image editing tasks typically adopt powerful generative diffusion models as the leading paradigm for real-world content editing. Meanwhile, although reinforcement learning (RL) methods such as Diffusion-DPO and Flow-GRPO have further improved generation quality, efficiently applying Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) to diffusion-based editing remains largely unexplored, due to a lack of scalable human-preference datasets and frameworks tailored to diverse editing needs. To fill this gap, we propose HP-Edit, a post-training framework for Human Preference-aligned Editing, and introduce RealPref-50K, a real-world dataset across eight common tasks and balancing common object editing. Specifically, HP-Edit leverages a small amount of human-preference scoring data and a pretrained visual large language model (VLM) to develop HP-Scorer--an automatic, human preference-aligned evaluator. We then use HP-Scorer both to efficiently build a scalable preference dataset and to serve as the reward function for post-training the editing model. We also introduce RealPref-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating real-world editing performance. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly enhances models such as Qwen-Image-Edit-2509, aligning their outputs more closely with human preference.
中文标题/摘要

LPO: Towards Accurate GUI Agent Interaction via Location Preference Optimization
Authors: Jiaqi Tang, Yu Xia, Yi-Feng Wu, Yuwei Hu, Yuhui Chen, Qing-Guo Chen, Xiaogang Xu, Xiangyu Wu, Hao Lu, Yanqing Ma, Shiyin Lu, Qifeng Chen
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-06-11T03:43:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T11:50:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The advent of autonomous agents is transforming interactions with Graphical User Interfaces (GUIs) by employing natural language as a powerful intermediary. Despite the predominance of Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) methods in current GUI agents for achieving spatial localization, these methods face substantial challenges due to their limited capacity to accurately perceive positional data. Existing strategies, such as reinforcement learning, often fail to assess positional accuracy effectively, thereby restricting their utility. In response, we introduce Location Preference Optimization (LPO), a novel approach that leverages locational data to optimize interaction preferences. LPO uses information entropy to predict interaction positions by focusing on zones rich in information. Besides, it further introduces a dynamic location reward function based on physical distance, reflecting the varying importance of interaction positions. Supported by Group Relative Preference Optimization (GRPO), LPO facilitates an extensive exploration of GUI environments and significantly enhances interaction precision. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate LPO's superior performance, achieving SOTA results across both offline benchmarks and real-world online evaluations. Our code will be made publicly available soon, at https://github.com/jqtangust/LPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LPO：基于位置偏好优化的精准图形用户界面智能体交互方法
自主智能体的兴起正通过自然语言作为高效中介，改变着与图形用户界面（GUI）的交互方式。尽管当前GUI智能体主要采用监督微调（SFT）方法实现空间定位，但这些方法因位置感知能力有限而面临显著挑战。现有策略（如强化学习）常难以有效评估位置精度，限制了其实用性。为此，我们提出位置偏好优化（LPO），这是一种利用位置数据优化交互偏好的新方法。LPO通过信息熵聚焦信息富集区域来预测交互位置，并进一步引入基于物理距离的动态位置奖励函数，以反映交互位置的重要性差异。在组相对偏好优化（GRPO）的支持下，LPO促进了对GUI环境的广泛探索，并显著提升了交互精度。综合实验表明LPO性能优越，在离线基准测试和真实在线评估中均达到最先进水平。代码即将公开于https://github.com/jqtangust/LPO。

This paper addresses the challenge of accurately localizing interaction points for GUI agents, noting that current supervised fine-tuning methods struggle with positional perception and reinforcement learning lacks effective accuracy assessment. The authors propose Location Preference Optimization (LPO), a novel method that uses information entropy to predict interaction positions by focusing on information-rich zones and incorporates a dynamic location reward function based on physical distance to reflect positional importance, supported by Group Relative Preference Optimization for enhanced exploration. Experimental results show that LPO achieves state-of-the-art performance on both offline benchmarks and real-world online evaluations, demonstrating superior interaction precision.
本文针对图形用户界面（GUI）代理在交互点精确定位上的挑战，指出当前监督微调方法在位置感知上存在局限，而强化学习则缺乏有效的准确性评估。作者提出了位置偏好优化（LPO）这一新方法，该方法利用信息熵聚焦信息丰富区域来预测交互位置，并引入基于物理距离的动态位置奖励函数以反映位置重要性，同时借助组相对偏好优化来促进环境探索。综合实验表明，LPO在离线基准测试和真实在线评估中均取得了最先进的性能，显著提升了交互精度。
LASER: Learning Active Sensing for Continuum Field Reconstruction
Authors: Huayu Deng, Jinghui Zhong, Xiangming Zhu, Yunbo Wang, Xiaokang Yang
First: 2026-04-21T11:36:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T11:36:09+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
High-fidelity measurements of continuum physical fields are essential for scientific discovery and engineering design but remain challenging under sparse and constrained sensing. Conventional reconstruction methods typically rely on fixed sensor layouts, which cannot adapt to evolving physical states. We propose LASER, a unified, closed-loop framework that formulates active sensing as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP). At its core, LASER employs a continuum field latent world model that captures the underlying physical dynamics and provides intrinsic reward feedback. This enables a reinforcement learning policy to simulate ''what-if'' sensing scenarios within a latent imagination space. By conditioning sensor movements on predicted latent states, LASER navigates toward potentially high-information regions beyond current observations. Our experiments demonstrate that LASER consistently outperforms static and offline-optimized strategies, achieving high-fidelity reconstruction under sparsity across diverse continuum fields.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LASER：面向连续场重建的主动感知学习框架
连续物理场的高保真测量对科学发现与工程设计至关重要，但在稀疏与受限感知条件下仍具挑战。传统重建方法通常依赖固定传感器布局，无法适应动态变化的物理状态。本文提出LASER，一个统一的闭环框架，将主动感知建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程。其核心是采用连续场潜在世界模型，该模型能捕捉底层物理动力学并提供内在奖励反馈，使强化学习策略能在潜在想象空间中模拟“假设性”感知场景。通过将传感器移动条件建立在预测潜在状态上，LASER可引导传感器向当前观测范围外的高信息潜力区域探索。实验表明，LASER在多种连续场中均优于静态与离线优化策略，在稀疏条件下实现了高保真重建。

Resource-aware Mixed-precision Quantization for Enhancing Deployability of Transformers for Time-series Forecasting on Embedded FPGAs
Authors: Tianheng Ling, Chao Qian, Gregor Schiele
First: 2024-10-04T10:12:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T10:27:28+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 8 figures, 6 tables, accepted by the 21st EAI International Conference on Mobile and Ubiquitous Systems: Computing, Networking and Services (MobiQuitous2024)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study addresses the deployment challenges of integer-only quantized Transformers on resource-constrained embedded FPGAs (Xilinx Spartan-7 XC7S15). We enhanced the flexibility of our VHDL template by introducing a selectable resource type for storing intermediate results across model layers, thereby breaking the deployment bottleneck by utilizing BRAM efficiently. Moreover, we developed a resource-aware mixed-precision quantization approach that enables researchers to explore hardware-level quantization strategies without requiring extensive expertise in Neural Architecture Search. This method provides accurate resource utilization estimates with a precision discrepancy as low as 3%, compared to actual deployment metrics. Compared to previous work, our approach has successfully facilitated the deployment of model configurations utilizing mixed-precision quantization, thus overcoming the limitations inherent in five previously non-deployable configurations with uniform quantization bitwidths. Consequently, this research enhances the applicability of Transformers in embedded systems, facilitating a broader range of Transformer-powered applications on edge devices.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向嵌入式FPGA时序预测的Transformer可部署性增强：资源感知混合精度量化方法

本研究旨在提升仅整数量化Transformer在资源受限嵌入式FPGA（如Xilinx Spartan-7）上的可部署性。方法上，通过引入具有可选中继存储资源类型的灵活VHDL模板，以及一种资源感知的混合精度量化方法，降低了硬件级优化对神经架构搜索专业知识的依赖。实验结果表明，该方法提供的资源利用率估计与实际部署指标误差低至3%，并成功部署了先前因均匀量化位宽而无法部署的模型配置，从而拓展了Transformer在嵌入式边缘设备中的应用范围。
Remote Rowhammer Attack using Adversarial Observations on Federated Learning Clients
Authors: Jinsheng Yuan, Yuhang Hao, Weisi Guo, Yun Wu, Chongyan Gu
First: 2025-05-09T17:27:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T09:43:38+00:00
Comments: Under review for IEEE Transactions on Dependable and Secure Computing
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated Learning (FL) has the potential for simultaneous global learning amongst a large number of parallel agents, enabling emerging AI such as LLMs to be trained across demographically diverse data. Central to this being efficient is the ability for FL to perform sparse gradient updates and remote direct memory access at the central server. Most of the research in FL security focuses on protecting data privacy at the edge client or in the communication channels between the client and server. Client-facing attacks on the server are less well investigated as the assumption is that a large collective of clients offer resilience. Here, we show that by attacking certain clients that lead to a high frequency repetitive memory update in the server, we can remote initiate a rowhammer attack on the server memory. For the first time, we do not need backdoor access to the server, and a reinforcement learning (RL) attacker can learn how to maximize server repetitive memory updates by manipulating the client's sensor observation. The consequence of the remote rowhammer attack is that we are able to achieve bit flips, which can corrupt the server memory. We demonstrate the feasibility of our attack using a large-scale FL automatic speech recognition (ASR) systems with sparse updates, our adversarial attacking agent can achieve around 70% repeated update rate (RUR) in the targeted server model, effectively inducing bit flips on server DRAM. The security implications are that can cause disruptions to learning or may inadvertently cause elevated privilege. This paves the way for further research on practical mitigation strategies in FL and hardware design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于联邦学习客户端对抗观测的远程Rowhammer攻击
联邦学习（FL）具备在大量并行代理间实现同步全局学习的潜力，使LLM等新兴AI技术能够基于多样化人口数据进行训练。其效率核心在于FL能够执行稀疏梯度更新及在中央服务器进行远程直接内存访问。现有FL安全研究多聚焦于边缘客户端或通信信道的数据隐私保护，而针对服务器的客户端攻击研究较少，因传统假设认为大规模客户端集群具备抗攻击韧性。本文首次证明：通过攻击特定客户端以触发服务器高频重复内存更新，可远程对服务器内存发起Rowhammer攻击。该方法无需服务器后门访问权限，强化学习攻击者可通过操控客户端传感器观测，学习如何最大化服务器重复内存更新。远程Rowhammer攻击可导致比特翻转，进而破坏服务器内存。我们在采用稀疏更新的大规模FL自动语音识别系统中验证了攻击可行性：对抗攻击代理能在目标服务器模型中实现约70%的重复更新率，有效诱发服务器DRAM比特翻转。其安全影响包括可能中断学习进程或意外引发权限提升，这为FL及硬件设计领域的实用化防御策略研究开辟了新路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the security vulnerabilities in Federated Learning (FL) systems, where prior research has focused on client-side privacy and communication channels, this paper investigates a novel remote attack on the server. The method employs a reinforcement learning (RL) attacker that manipulates sensor observations on selected clients to induce high-frequency repetitive memory updates at the server, thereby initiating a rowhammer attack without requiring direct server access. Experimental results on a large-scale FL automatic speech recognition system demonstrate that the adversarial agent achieves approximately 70% repeated update rate, effectively causing bit flips in server DRAM, which can corrupt memory, disrupt learning, or lead to privilege escalation.
本文的动机源于联邦学习（FL）系统中的安全漏洞，以往研究多关注客户端隐私和通信安全，而本文则探索了一种针对服务器的新型远程攻击。方法上，采用强化学习攻击者操纵选定客户端的传感器观测，以在服务器端引发高频重复内存更新，从而无需直接访问服务器即可发起行锤攻击。实验结果表明，在大规模FL自动语音识别系统中，该对抗性代理能实现约70%的重复更新率，有效导致服务器DRAM发生位翻转，可能破坏内存、中断学习或引发权限提升。
TROJail: Trajectory-Level Optimization for Multi-Turn Large Language Model Jailbreaks with Process Rewards
Authors: Xiqiao Xiong, Ouxiang Li, Zhuo Liu, Moxin Li, Wentao Shi, Fengbin Zhu, Qifan Wang, Fuli Feng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-12-08T17:42:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T08:41:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models have seen widespread adoption, yet they remain vulnerable to multi-turn jailbreak attacks, threatening their safe deployment. This has led to the task of training automated multi-turn attackers to probe model safety vulnerabilities. However, existing approaches typically rely on turn-level optimization, which is insufficient for learning long-term attack strategies. To bridge this gap, we formulate this task as a multi-turn reinforcement learning problem, directly optimizing the harmfulness of the final-turn response as the outcome reward. To address the sparse supervision of the outcome reward, we introduce TROJail, which employs two process rewards to evaluate the utility of intermediate prompts and integrate them into advantage estimation. These rewards (1) penalize overly harmful prompts that trigger the model's refusal mechanism, and (2) encourage steering the semantic relevance of responses toward the targeted harmful content. Experimental results show improved attack success rates across multiple models and benchmarks, highlighting the effectiveness of our approach. The code is available at https://github.com/xxiqiao/TROJail. Warning: This paper contains examples of harmful content.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TROJail：基于过程奖励的多轮大语言模型越狱轨迹级优化方法
大语言模型已获广泛应用，但仍易受多轮越狱攻击威胁，影响其安全部署。为此，训练自动化多轮攻击器以探测模型安全漏洞成为重要任务。现有方法通常依赖轮次级优化，难以学习长期攻击策略。为弥补这一不足，我们将该任务构建为多轮强化学习问题，直接以最终轮次回复的危害性作为结果奖励进行优化。针对结果奖励监督稀疏的问题，本文提出TROJail方法，通过引入两个过程奖励来评估中间提示的效用并整合至优势估计中：其一对触发模型拒绝机制的过度有害提示进行惩罚，其二引导回复的语义相关性朝向目标有害内容。实验结果表明，该方法在多个模型与基准测试中均提升了攻击成功率，验证了其有效性。代码发布于https://github.com/xxiqiao/TROJail。注：本文包含有害内容示例。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the vulnerability of large language models to multi-turn jailbreak attacks and the limitations of turn-level optimization in learning long-term strategies, this paper formulates the task as a multi-turn reinforcement learning problem, directly optimizing the final harmful response. The method, TROJail, introduces two process rewards to address sparse outcome supervision: one penalizes overly harmful prompts that trigger refusal, and another encourages steering response relevance toward targeted harmful content. Experimental results demonstrate improved attack success rates across multiple models and benchmarks, validating the approach's effectiveness.
针对大语言模型在多轮越狱攻击中的脆弱性以及逐轮优化在长期策略学习上的不足，本文将该任务构建为多轮强化学习问题，直接优化最终的有害响应。所提出的TROJail方法引入了两个过程奖励以解决结果监督稀疏的问题：一个惩罚触发模型拒绝机制的过度有害提示，另一个鼓励引导响应语义相关性朝向目标有害内容。实验结果表明，该方法在多个模型和基准测试中提高了攻击成功率，验证了其有效性。
Reasoning-Aware AIGC Detection via Alignment and Reinforcement
Authors: Zhao Wang, Max Xiong, Jianxun Lian, Zhicheng Dou
First: 2026-04-21T07:29:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T07:29:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid advancement and widespread adoption of Large Language Models (LLMs) have elevated the need for reliable AI-generated content (AIGC) detection, which remains challenging as models evolve. We introduce AIGC-text-bank, a comprehensive multi-domain dataset with diverse LLM sources and authorship scenarios, and propose REVEAL, a detection framework that generates interpretable reasoning chains before classification. Our approach uses a two-stage training strategy: supervised fine-tuning to establish reasoning capabilities, followed by reinforcement learning to improve accuracy, improve logical consistency, and reduce hallucinations. Extensive experiments show that REVEAL achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple benchmarks, offering a robust and transparent solution for AIGC detection. The project is open-source at https://aka.ms/reveal

Quantum spatial best-arm identification via quantum walks
Authors: Tomoki Yamagami, Etsuo Segawa, Takatomo Mihana, André Röhm, Atsushi Uchida, Ryoichi Horisaki
First: 2025-09-07T01:53:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T07:28:56+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum reinforcement learning has emerged as a framework combining quantum computation with sequential decision-making, and applications to the multi-armed bandit (MAB) problem have been reported. The graph bandit problem extends the MAB setting by introducing spatial constraints, where the accessibility of arms is restricted by graph connectivity, yet quantum approaches to this setting remain limited. In this paper, we formulate best-arm identification in graph bandits and propose a quantum algorithmic framework, termed Quantum Spatial Best-Arm Identification (QSBAI), which is applicable to general graph structures. This framework uses quantum walks to encode superpositions over graph-constrained actions, thereby extending amplitude amplification and generalizing the quantum BAI algorithm via Szegedy's walk framework. We focus our theoretical analysis on complete and bipartite graphs, deriving the maximal success probability of identifying the best arm and the time step at which it is achieved. Our results clarify how quantum-walk-based search can be adapted to structurally constrained decision problems and provide a foundation for quantum best-arm identification in graph-structured environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于量子行走的量子空间最优臂识别
量子强化学习已成为结合量子计算与序列决策的框架，其在多臂老虎机问题中的应用已有报道。图老虎机问题通过引入空间约束扩展了MAB设定，其中臂的可访问性受限于图连通性，但针对该设定的量子方法仍较为有限。本文构建了图老虎机中的最优臂识别问题，并提出一种适用于通用图结构的量子算法框架——量子空间最优臂识别。该框架利用量子行走编码图约束动作的叠加态，从而扩展振幅放大技术，并通过Szegedy行走框架推广了量子BAI算法。理论分析聚焦于完全图与二分图，推导了识别最优臂的最大成功概率及其实现的时间步。研究结果阐明了基于量子行走的搜索如何适应结构约束的决策问题，并为图结构环境中的量子最优臂识别奠定了基础。

Motivated by the need to extend quantum reinforcement learning to spatially constrained decision problems like graph bandits, this paper proposes a quantum algorithmic framework called Quantum Spatial Best-Arm Identification (QSBAI). The method leverages quantum walks to encode superpositions over graph-accessible actions, adapting amplitude amplification and generalizing quantum best-arm identification via Szegedy's walk framework. Experimental analysis on complete and bipartite graphs derives the maximal success probability for identifying the best arm and the optimal time step, demonstrating how quantum-walk-based search can be tailored to graph-structured environments.

RL-ABC: Reinforcement Learning for Accelerator Beamline Control
Authors: Anwar Ibrahim, Fedor Ratnikov, Maxim Kaledin, Alexey Petrenko, Denis Derkach
First: 2026-04-21T06:52:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:52:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Particle accelerator beamline optimization is a high-dimensional control problem traditionally requiring significant expert intervention. We present RLABC (Reinforcement Learning for Accelerator Beamline Control), an open-source Python framework that automatically transforms standard Elegant beamline configurations into reinforcement learning environments. RLABC integrates with the widely-used Elegant beam dynamics simulation code via SDDS-based interfaces, enabling researchers to apply modern RL algorithms to beamline optimization with minimal RL-specific development. The main contribution is a general methodology for formulating beamline tuning as a Markov decision process: RLABC automatically preprocesses lattice files to insert diagnostic watch points before each tunable element, constructs a 57-dimensional state representation from beam statistics, covariance information, and aperture constraints, and provides a configurable reward function for transmission optimization. The framework supports multiple RL algorithms through Stable-Baselines3 compatibility and implements stage learning strategies for improved training efficiency. Validation on a test beamline derived from the VEPP-5 injection complex (37 control parameters across 11 quadrupoles and 4 dipoles) demonstrates that the framework successfully enables RL-based optimization, with a Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient agent achieving 70.3\% particle transmission -- performance matching established methods such as differential evolution. The framework's stage learning capability allows decomposition of complex optimization problems into manageable subproblems, improving training efficiency. The complete framework, including configuration files and example notebooks, is available as open-source software to facilitate adoption and further research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-ABC：基于强化学习的加速器束流线控制
粒子加速器束流线优化是一个传统上需要大量专家干预的高维控制问题。本文提出RLABC（基于强化学习的加速器束流线控制框架），这是一个开源Python框架，能够自动将标准Elegant束流线配置转换为强化学习环境。RLABC通过基于SDDS的接口与广泛使用的Elegant束流动力学模拟代码集成，使研究人员能够以最少的强化学习专用开发工作，将现代强化学习算法应用于束流线优化。 主要贡献在于提出将束流线调谐建模为马尔可夫决策过程的通用方法：RLABC自动预处理晶格文件，在每个可调元件前插入诊断监测点；基于束流统计量、协方差信息和孔径约束构建57维状态表示；并提供可配置的奖励函数用于传输优化。该框架通过Stable-Baselines3兼容性支持多种强化学习算法，并实现了分阶段学习策略以提升训练效率。 在基于VEPP-5注入复合体衍生的测试束流线（涵盖11个四极磁铁和4个二极磁铁的37个控制参数）上的验证表明，该框架成功实现了基于强化学习的优化，深度确定性策略梯度智能体实现了70.3%的粒子传输率——其性能与差分进化等成熟方法相当。框架的分阶段学习能力可将复杂优化问题分解为可管理的子问题，从而提升训练效率。完整框架（包括配置文件和示例笔记本）已作为开源软件发布，以促进实际应用和进一步研究。

ARM: Advantage Reward Modeling for Long-Horizon Manipulation
Authors: Yiming Mao, Zixi Yu, Weixin Mao, Yinhao Li, Qirui Hu, Zihan Lan, Minzhao Zhu, Hua Chen
First: 2026-04-03T13:45:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:50:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-horizon robotic manipulation remains challenging for reinforcement learning (RL) because sparse rewards provide limited guidance for credit assignment. Practical policy improvement thus relies on richer intermediate supervision, such as dense progress rewards, which are costly to obtain and ill-suited to non-monotonic behaviors such as backtracking and recovery. To address this, we propose Advantage Reward Modeling (ARM), a framework that shifts from hard-to-quantify absolute progress to estimating relative advantage. We introduce a cost-effective tri-state labeling strategy -- Progressive, Regressive, and Stagnant -- that reduces human cognitive overhead while ensuring high cross-annotator consistency. By training on these intuitive signals, ARM enables automated progress annotation for both complete demonstrations and fragmented DAgger-style data. Integrating ARM into an offline RL pipeline allows for adaptive action-reward reweighting, effectively filtering suboptimal samples. Our approach achieves a 99.4% success rate on a challenging long-horizon towel-folding task, demonstrating improved stability and data efficiency over current VLA baselines with near-zero human intervention during policy training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARM：面向长时程操作的优势奖励建模
长时程机器人操作对强化学习仍具挑战性，稀疏奖励难以支撑有效的信度分配。实际策略改进需依赖更丰富的中间监督信号（如稠密进度奖励），但这类信号获取成本高，且不适用于回溯、恢复等非单调行为。为此，我们提出优势奖励建模框架，将难以量化的绝对进度评估转为相对优势估计。我们引入低成本的三态标注策略——进展态、回归态、停滞态，在降低人工认知负荷的同时保证标注者间的高一致性。基于这些直观信号训练后，ARM能对完整演示数据和碎片化DAgger式数据实现自动化进度标注。将ARM集成至离线强化学习流程中，可实现自适应动作奖励重加权，有效过滤次优样本。在具挑战性的长时程毛巾折叠任务中，本方法达到99.4%成功率，相较于当前视觉语言动作基线，在策略训练阶段近乎零人工干预的情况下，展现出更优的稳定性与数据效率。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sparse rewards in long-horizon robotic manipulation by proposing Advantage Reward Modeling (ARM), which shifts from absolute progress to estimating relative advantage using a cost-effective tri-state labeling strategy (Progressive, Regressive, Stagnant) to reduce human annotation burden. This method enables automated progress annotation for demonstrations and fragmented data, and when integrated into an offline RL pipeline, it allows adaptive reweighting to filter suboptimal samples. Experimental results show ARM achieves a 99.4% success rate on a towel-folding task, outperforming visual-language action baselines in stability and data efficiency with minimal human intervention.
本文针对长时程机器人操作中稀疏奖励带来的挑战，提出了优势奖励建模（ARM），通过从绝对进度估计转向相对优势估计，采用一种低成本的三态标注策略（进步、退步、停滞）来降低人工标注负担。该方法能对完整演示和碎片化数据进行自动进度标注，并集成到离线强化学习流程中，通过自适应重加权过滤次优样本。实验结果表明，ARM在毛巾折叠任务上实现了99.4%的成功率，相比现有视觉语言动作基线，在稳定性和数据效率上表现更优，且策略训练期间几乎无需人工干预。
Bootstrapping Code Translation with Weighted Multilanguage Exploration
Authors: Yuhan Wu, Huan Zhang, Wei Cheng, Chen Shen, Jingyue Yang, Wei Hu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-07T01:56:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:44:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted in the 64th Annual Meeting of the Association for Computational Linguistics (ACL 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Code translation across multiple programming languages is essential yet challenging due to two vital obstacles: scarcity of parallel data paired with executable test oracles, and optimization imbalance when handling diverse language pairs. We propose BootTrans, a bootstrapping method that resolves both obstacles. Its key idea is to leverage the functional invariance and cross-lingual portability of test suites, adapting abundant pivot-language unit tests to serve as universal verification oracles for multilingual reinforcement learning (RL) training. Our method introduces a dual-pool architecture with seed and exploration pools to progressively expand training data via execution-guided experience collection. Furthermore, we design a language-aware weighting mechanism that dynamically prioritizes harder translation directions based on relative performance across sibling languages, mitigating optimization imbalance. Extensive experiments on the HumanEval-X and TransCoder-Test benchmarks demonstrate substantial improvements over baseline LLMs across all translation directions, with ablation studies validating the effectiveness of both bootstrapping and weighting components.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于加权多语言探索的代码翻译自举方法
跨多编程语言的代码翻译至关重要，但面临两大关键挑战：兼具可执行测试用例的平行数据稀缺，以及处理不同语言对时的优化失衡。我们提出BootTrans自举方法，通过利用测试套件的功能不变性与跨语言可移植性，将丰富的枢轴语言单元测试适配为多语言强化学习训练的通用验证机制。该方法采用种子池与探索池的双池架构，通过执行引导的经验收集逐步扩展训练数据。此外，我们设计了语言感知加权机制，根据兄弟语言间的相对性能动态优先处理更难翻译方向，从而缓解优化失衡问题。在HumanEval-X和TransCoder-Test基准上的大量实验表明，该方法在所有翻译方向上均显著优于基线大语言模型，消融研究验证了自举与加权组件的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the scarcity of parallel data with executable test oracles and the optimization imbalance in multilingual code translation, this paper proposes BootTrans, a bootstrapping method that leverages the functional invariance of test suites to adapt pivot-language unit tests as universal verification oracles for reinforcement learning training. The method employs a dual-pool architecture to progressively expand training data via execution-guided experience collection and incorporates a language-aware weighting mechanism to dynamically prioritize harder translation directions. Experimental results on HumanEval-X and TransCoder-Test benchmarks show substantial improvements over baseline large language models across all translation directions, with ablations confirming the effectiveness of both bootstrapping and weighting components.
本文针对多语言代码翻译中并行数据稀缺与测试预言不足以及优化不平衡的挑战，提出了BootTrans方法，其核心是利用测试套件的功能不变性，将丰富的枢纽语言单元测试适配为多语言强化学习的通用验证预言。该方法采用种子池和探索池的双池架构，通过执行引导的经验收集逐步扩展训练数据，并设计了语言感知加权机制，根据兄弟语言间的相对性能动态优先处理较难的翻译方向以缓解优化失衡。在HumanEval-X和TransCoder-Test基准上的大量实验表明，该方法在所有翻译方向上均显著优于基线大语言模型，消融研究验证了自举和加权组件的有效性。
The Rise of Verbal Tics in Large Language Models: A Systematic Analysis Across Frontier Models
Authors: Shuai Wu, Xue Li, Yanna Feng, Yufang Li, Zhijun Wang, Ran Wang
First: 2026-04-21T06:43:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:43:01+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 17 figures, 8 tables. Technical report
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As Large Language Models (LLMs) continue to evolve through alignment techniques such as Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and Constitutional AI, a growing and increasingly conspicuous phenomenon has emerged: the proliferation of verbal tics -- repetitive, formulaic linguistic patterns that pervade model outputs. These range from sycophantic openers ("That's a great question!", "Awesome!") to pseudo-empathetic affirmations ("I completely understand your concern", "I'm right here to catch you") and overused vocabulary ("delve", "tapestry", "nuanced"). In this paper, we present a systematic analysis of the verbal tic phenomenon across eight state-of-the-art LLMs: GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.7, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Grok 4.2, Doubao-Seed-2.0-pro, Kimi K2.5, DeepSeek V3.2, and MiMo-V2-Pro. Utilizing a custom evaluation framework for standardized API-based evaluation, we assess 10,000 prompts across 10 task categories in both English and Chinese, yielding 160,000 model responses. We introduce the Verbal Tic Index (VTI), a composite metric quantifying tic prevalence, and analyze its correlation with sycophancy, lexical diversity, and human-perceived naturalness. Our findings reveal significant inter-model variation: Gemini 3.1 Pro exhibits the highest VTI (0.590), while DeepSeek V3.2 achieves the lowest (0.295). We further demonstrate that verbal tics accumulate over multi-turn conversations, are amplified in subjective tasks, and show distinct cross-lingual patterns. Human evaluation (N = 120) confirms a strong inverse relationship between sycophancy and perceived naturalness (r = -0.87, p < 0.001). These results underscore the "alignment tax" of current training paradigms and highlight the urgent need for more authentic human-AI interaction frameworks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型言语重复现象的系统性分析：前沿模型的跨模型研究
随着大语言模型通过人类反馈强化学习和宪法人工智能等对齐技术持续演进，一个日益显著的现象逐渐浮现：言语重复——即模型输出中普遍存在的重复性、公式化语言模式。这些模式涵盖奉承式开场白（"这个问题很棒！"、"太棒了！"）、伪共情式肯定（"我完全理解您的担忧"、"我随时在此为您提供支持"）以及过度使用的词汇（"深入探讨"、"交织画卷"、"微妙差异"）。本文对八款前沿大语言模型的言语重复现象展开系统性分析，包括GPT-5.4、Claude Opus 4.7、Gemini 3.1 Pro、Grok 4.2、豆包-Seed-2.0-pro、Kimi K2.5、DeepSeek V3.2和MiMo-V2-Pro。通过构建基于标准化API评估的定制框架，我们在中英文双语环境下对10个任务类别的1万条提示进行测试，获得16万条模型响应。我们提出言语重复指数这一复合指标来量化重复现象普遍性，并分析其与奉承倾向、词汇多样性及人类感知自然度的相关性。研究发现：Gemini 3.1 Pro的VTI值最高（0.590），DeepSeek V3.2最低（0.295）；言语重复在多轮对话中持续累积，在主观性任务中表现更显著，且呈现跨语言差异模式。人类评估（N=120）证实奉承倾向与感知自然度呈强负相关（r=-0.87, p<0.001）。这些结果揭示了当前训练范式存在的"对齐代价"，凸显了构建更真实人机交互框架的迫切需求。
Summary / 总结
This study is motivated by the observation that advanced Large Language Models (LLMs), trained with alignment techniques like RLHF, increasingly produce repetitive and formulaic phrases known as verbal tics, such as sycophantic openers and overused vocabulary. The authors systematically analyze this phenomenon across eight frontier LLMs by developing a custom evaluation framework and a Verbal Tic Index (VTI) metric, testing 10,000 prompts across 10 tasks in English and Chinese to generate 160,000 responses. Key experimental results show significant variation in tic prevalence among models, with Gemini 3.1 Pro having the highest VTI and DeepSeek V3.2 the lowest, and reveal that tics accumulate in multi-turn conversations, are more common in subjective tasks, and correlate strongly with reduced human-perceived naturalness, highlighting an 'alignment tax' in current training methods.
本研究源于观察到采用人类反馈强化学习等对齐技术训练的大型语言模型，其输出中日益出现重复、公式化的语言模式，即言语抽搐，如奉承性开场白和过度使用的词汇。作者通过构建定制评估框架和言语抽搐指数（VTI）指标，对八个前沿大模型进行了系统分析，在英语和中文的10个任务类别上测试了1万个提示，生成了16万个响应。主要实验结果表明，不同模型的抽搐现象存在显著差异，其中Gemini 3.1 Pro的VTI最高，而DeepSeek V3.2最低；研究还发现抽搐在多轮对话中累积，在主观任务中更明显，且与人类感知的自然度呈强负相关，这揭示了当前训练范式带来的'对齐代价'。
Pareto Optimization with Robust Evaluation for Noisy Subset Selection
Authors: Yiheng Xu, Danxuan Liu, Bin Zhang, Weiyong Yang, Chao Qian
First: 2025-01-12T14:04:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:35:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Subset selection is a fundamental problem in combinatorial optimization, which has a wide range of applications such as influence maximization and sparse regression. The goal is to select a subset of limited size from a ground set in order to maximize a given objective function. However, the evaluation of the objective function in real-world scenarios is often noisy. Previous algorithms, including the greedy algorithm and multi-objective evolutionary algorithms POSS and PONSS, either struggle in noisy environments or consume excessive computational resources. In this paper, we focus on the noisy subset selection problem with a cardinality constraint, where the evaluation of a subset is noisy. We propose a novel approach based on Pareto Optimization with Robust Evaluation for noisy subset selection (PORE), which maximizes a robust evaluation function and minimizes the subset size simultaneously. PORE can efficiently identify well-structured solutions and handle computational resources, addressing the limitations observed in PONSS. Our experiments, conducted on real-world datasets for influence maximization and sparse regression, demonstrate that PORE significantly outperforms previous methods, including the classical greedy algorithm, POSS, and PONSS. Further validation through ablation studies confirms the effectiveness of our robust evaluation function.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于鲁棒评估的噪声子集选择帕累托优化
子集选择是组合优化中的基础问题，在影响力最大化和稀疏回归等领域有广泛应用。其目标是从基础集合中选取规模有限的子集，以最大化给定目标函数。然而，实际场景中目标函数的评估常受噪声干扰。现有算法（如贪心算法、多目标进化算法POSS和PONSS）在噪声环境中表现不佳或计算资源消耗过大。本文聚焦带基数约束的噪声子集选择问题，提出基于鲁棒评估的帕累托优化方法（PORE），同步最大化鲁棒评估函数并最小化子集规模。PORE能高效识别结构良好的解并优化计算资源，克服了PONSS的局限性。在影响力最大化和稀疏回归的真实数据集实验中，PORE显著优于传统贪心算法、POSS和PONSS。消融实验进一步验证了鲁棒评估函数的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the prevalence of noisy objective evaluations in real-world subset selection problems like influence maximization and sparse regression, this paper introduces Pareto Optimization with Robust Evaluation (PORE) to address the limitations of prior methods such as greedy algorithms, POSS, and PONSS, which either perform poorly under noise or are computationally expensive. The method simultaneously maximizes a robust evaluation function and minimizes subset size through Pareto optimization, efficiently identifying well-structured solutions while managing computational resources. Experimental results on real-world datasets for influence maximization and sparse regression show that PORE significantly outperforms previous approaches, with ablation studies confirming the effectiveness of the robust evaluation function.
针对现实世界中影响力最大化和稀疏回归等子集选择问题常存在目标函数评估噪声的挑战，本文提出了基于鲁棒评估的帕累托优化方法（PORE），以解决贪婪算法、POSS和PONSS等先前方法在噪声环境下性能不佳或计算资源消耗过大的局限。该方法通过帕累托优化同时最大化鲁棒评估函数并最小化子集规模，从而高效识别结构良好的解并管理计算资源。在影响力最大化和稀疏回归的真实数据集上的实验表明，PORE显著优于先前方法，消融研究进一步验证了其鲁棒评估函数的有效性。
Temp-R1: A Unified Autonomous Agent for Complex Temporal KGQA via Reverse Curriculum Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhaoyan Gong, Zhiqiang Liu, Songze Li, Xiaoke Guo, Yuanxiang Liu, Xinle Deng, Zhizhen Liu, Lei Liang, Huajun Chen, Wen Zhang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-26T09:23:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T06:22:33+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Temporal Knowledge Graph Question Answering (TKGQA) is inherently challenging, as it requires sophisticated reasoning over dynamic facts with multi-hop dependencies and complex temporal constraints. Existing methods rely on fixed workflows and expensive closed-source APIs, limiting flexibility and scalability. We propose Temp-R1, the first autonomous end-to-end agent for TKGQA trained through reinforcement learning. To address cognitive overload in single-action reasoning, we expand the action space with specialized internal actions alongside external action. To prevent shortcut learning on simple questions, we introduce reverse curriculum learning that trains on difficult questions first, forcing the development of sophisticated reasoning before transferring to easier cases. Our 8B-parameter Temp-R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance on MultiTQ and TimelineKGQA, improving 19.8% over strong baselines on complex questions. Our work establishes a new paradigm for autonomous temporal reasoning agents. The code is available at https://github.com/zjukg/Temp-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Temp-R1：基于逆向课程强化学习的复杂时序知识图谱问答统一自主智能体
时序知识图谱问答（TKGQA）因其需要对具有多跳依赖和复杂时序约束的动态事实进行精细推理而具有本质挑战性。现有方法依赖固定流程和昂贵的闭源API，限制了灵活性与可扩展性。我们提出首个通过强化学习训练的端到端自主TKGQA智能体Temp-R1。为解决单步推理中的认知过载问题，我们在外部动作基础上扩展了包含专用内部动作的动作空间。为避免简单问题上的捷径学习，我们引入逆向课程学习机制，优先训练困难问题，迫使模型在迁移至简单案例前先发展出复杂推理能力。参数量为80亿的Temp-R1在MultiTQ和TimelineKGQA数据集上取得最先进性能，在复杂问题上较基线模型提升19.8%。本研究为自主时序推理智能体确立了新范式。代码已开源：https://github.com/zjukg/Temp-R1。

Reinforcement Learning Enabled Adaptive Multi-Task Control for Bipedal Soccer Robots
Authors: Yulai Zhang, Yinrong Zhang, Ting Wu, Linqi Ye
First: 2026-04-21T05:27:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T05:27:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing bipedal football robots in dynamiccombat environments presents challenges related to motionstability and deep coupling of multiple tasks, as well ascontrol switching issues between different states such as up-right walking and fall recovery. To address these problems,this paper proposes a modular reinforcement learning (RL)framework for achieving adaptive multi-task control. Firstly,this framework combines an open-loop feedforward oscilla-tor with a reinforcement learning-based feedback residualstrategy, effectively separating the generation of basic gaitsfrom complex football actions. Secondly, a posture-driven statemachine is introduced, clearly switching between the ballseeking and kicking network (BSKN) and the fall recoverynetwork (FRN), fundamentally preventing state interference.The FRN is efficiently trained through a progressive forceattenuation curriculum learning strategy. The architecture wasverified in Unity simulations of bipedal robots, demonstratingexcellent spatial adaptability-reliably finding and kicking theball even in restricted corner scenarios-and rapid autonomousfall recovery (with an average recovery time of 0.715 seconds).This ensures seamless and stable operation in complex multi-task environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习驱动的双足足球机器人自适应多任务控制
在动态对抗环境中开发双足足球机器人面临运动稳定性、多任务深度耦合以及直立行走与跌倒恢复等不同状态间控制切换的挑战。为此，本文提出一种模块化强化学习框架以实现自适应多任务控制。该框架首先将开环前馈振荡器与基于强化学习的反馈残差策略相结合，有效分离基础步态生成与复杂足球动作；其次引入姿态驱动的状态机，清晰切换寻球踢球网络与跌倒恢复网络，从根本上防止状态干扰。跌倒恢复网络通过渐进式力衰减课程学习策略高效训练。该架构在双足机器人Unity仿真中验证，展现出卓越的空间适应性——即使在受限角落场景也能可靠寻球踢球，以及快速自主跌倒恢复能力（平均恢复时间0.715秒），确保复杂多任务环境中的无缝稳定运行。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of motion stability, multi-task coupling, and control switching in bipedal soccer robots operating in dynamic environments. It proposes a modular reinforcement learning framework that combines an open-loop feedforward oscillator with an RL-based feedback residual strategy to decouple basic gait generation from complex football actions, alongside a posture-driven state machine to switch between ball-seeking/kicking and fall recovery networks without interference. Experimental validation in Unity simulations shows the approach enables reliable ball finding and kicking in constrained spaces and achieves rapid autonomous fall recovery with an average time of 0.715 seconds, ensuring stable performance in multi-task scenarios.
