Multi-Gait Learning for Humanoid Robots Using Reinforcement Learning with Selective Adversarial Motion Prior
Authors: Yuanye Wu, Keyi Wang, Linqi Ye, Boyang Xing
First: 2026-04-21T05:26:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T05:26:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning diverse locomotion skills for humanoid robots in a unified reinforcement learning framework remains challenging due to the conflicting requirements of stability and dynamic expressiveness across different gaits. We present a multi-gait learning approach that enables a humanoid robot to master five distinct gaits -- walking, goose-stepping, running, stair climbing, and jumping -- using a consistent policy structure, action space, and reward formulation. The key contribution is a selective Adversarial Motion Prior (AMP) strategy: AMP is applied to periodic, stability-critical gaits (walking, goose-stepping, stair climbing) where it accelerates convergence and suppresses erratic behavior, while being deliberately omitted for highly dynamic gaits (running, jumping) where its regularization would over-constrain the motion. Policies are trained via PPO with domain randomization in simulation and deployed on a physical 12-DOF humanoid robot through zero-shot sim-to-real transfer. Quantitative comparisons demonstrate that selective AMP outperforms a uniform AMP policy across all five gaits, achieving faster convergence, lower tracking error, and higher success rates on stability-focused gaits without sacrificing the agility required for dynamic ones.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于选择性对抗运动先验强化学习的人形机器人多步态学习
在人形机器人的统一强化学习框架中学习多样化运动技能仍具挑战，主要源于不同步态对稳定性与动态表现力的冲突需求。本研究提出一种多步态学习方法，使机器人通过一致策略结构、动作空间与奖励机制掌握行走、正步、奔跑、爬梯和跳跃五种步态。核心创新在于选择性对抗运动先验策略：对周期性高稳定性步态（行走/正步/爬梯）应用AMP以加速收敛并抑制异常行为，而对高动态步态（奔跑/跳跃）则刻意省略AMP以避免过度约束运动。策略通过PPO算法结合领域随机化在仿真中训练，并基于零样本仿真到现实迁移部署于12自由度实体机器人。定量对比表明：选择性AMP策略在五项步态上均优于统一AMP策略，在稳定性步态上实现更快收敛、更低跟踪误差与更高成功率，同时保持动态步态所需的敏捷性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enabling humanoid robots to learn multiple locomotion gaits within a single reinforcement learning framework, where stability and dynamic expressiveness often conflict. The proposed method employs a selective Adversarial Motion Prior (AMP) strategy: AMP is applied to periodic, stability-critical gaits like walking and stair climbing to accelerate convergence and reduce erratic behavior, but is omitted for highly dynamic gaits such as running and jumping to avoid over-constraining motion. Using PPO with domain randomization in simulation, the approach was successfully transferred zero-shot to a physical 12-DOF humanoid robot, demonstrating that selective AMP outperforms uniform AMP across five gaits with faster convergence, lower tracking error, and higher success rates on stability-focused tasks while preserving agility for dynamic movements.
本文针对人形机器人在单一强化学习框架中学习多种步态时稳定性和动态表现力相互冲突的挑战，提出了一种选择性对抗运动先验方法。该方法对周期性、稳定性关键的步态（如行走和爬楼梯）应用AMP以加速收敛并抑制异常行为，而对高度动态的步态（如奔跑和跳跃）则有意省略AMP以避免过度约束运动。通过PPO算法结合仿真中的领域随机化进行策略训练，并零样本迁移到物理12自由度人形机器人上，实验结果表明，选择性AMP在五种步态上均优于统一AMP策略，实现了更快的收敛速度、更低的跟踪误差，并在稳定性任务中取得更高成功率，同时保持了动态步态的敏捷性。
OLLM: Options-based Large Language Models
Authors: Shashank Sharma, Janina Hoffmann, Vinay Namboodiri
First: 2026-04-21T04:59:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:59:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Options LLM (OLLM), a simple, general method that replaces the single next-token prediction of standard LLMs with a \textit{set of learned options} for the next token, indexed by a discrete latent variable. Instead of relying on temperature or sampling heuristics to induce diversity, OLLM models variation explicitly: a small latent space parametrizes multiple plausible next-token options which can be selected or searched by a downstream policy. Architecturally, OLLM is a lightweight "plug-in" that inserts two layers: an encoder and a decoder, before the output head, allowing almost any pretrained LLM to be converted with minimal additional parameters. We apply OLLM to a 1.7B-parameter backbone (only $1.56\%$ of parameters trainable) trained on OpenMathReasoning and evaluated on OmniMath. The SOTA LoRA-adapted baselines peak at $51\%$ final answer correctness, while OLLM's option set allows up to $\sim 70\%$ under optimal latent selection. We then train a compact policy in the latent space that emits latents to control generation. Operating in a low-dimensional option space makes reward optimization far more sample-efficient and substantially reduces common misalignments (e.g., language switching or degenerate reasoning), as the policy is constrained to options learned during SFT. Crucially, this alignment arises from model structure rather than additional KL or handcrafted alignment losses. Our results demonstrate that optionized next-token modeling enhances controllability, robustness, and efficiency in math reasoning, and highlight latent-space policy learning as a promising direction for reinforcement learning in LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OLLM：基于选项的大型语言模型
我们提出选项化大型语言模型（OLLM），这是一种简洁通用的方法，通过由离散隐变量索引的\textit{一组学习所得选项}替代标准LLM的单次下一词元预测。OLLM无需依赖温度调节或采样启发式方法即可显式建模多样性：其小型隐空间参数化多个合理的下一词元选项，可供下游策略进行选择或搜索。在架构层面，OLLM作为轻量级“插件”在输出层前插入编码器与解码器两层结构，能以极少的附加参数将绝大多数预训练LLM进行转化。我们在17亿参数骨干模型（仅$1.56\%$参数可训练）上应用OLLM，基于OpenMathReasoning训练并在OmniMath评估。经LoRA适配的基线模型最高仅达$51\%$最终答案准确率，而OLLM的选项集在最优隐变量选择下可实现约$70\%$准确率。我们进一步在隐空间训练紧凑策略以发射隐变量控制生成。低维选项空间的操作使奖励优化的样本效率显著提升，并大幅减少常见失调现象（如语言切换或退化推理），因为策略被约束在监督微调阶段学习的选项范围内。关键在于，这种对齐性源于模型结构而非额外的KL散度或人工设计的对齐损失。实验结果表明：选项化下一词元建模能增强数学推理的可控性、鲁棒性与效率，同时凸显隐空间策略学习作为LLM强化学习的重要发展方向。

The method replaces standard next-token prediction with a set of learned options indexed by a discrete latent variable, implemented via lightweight encoder and decoder layers added to pretrained LLMs, requiring minimal trainable parameters. FaithLens: Detecting and Explaining Faithfulness Hallucination
Authors: Shuzheng Si, Qingyi Wang, Haozhe Zhao, Yuzhuo Bai, Guanqiao Chen, Kangyang Luo, Gang Chen, Fanchao Qi, Minjia Zhang, Baobao Chang, Maosong Sun
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-12-23T09:20:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:28:11+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 (Findings)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recognizing whether outputs from large language models (LLMs) contain faithfulness hallucination is crucial for real-world applications, e.g., retrieval-augmented generation and summarization. In this paper, we introduce FaithLens, a cost-efficient and effective faithfulness hallucination detection model that can jointly provide binary predictions and corresponding explanations to improve trustworthiness. To achieve this, we first synthesize training data with explanations via advanced LLMs and apply a well-defined data filtering strategy to ensure label correctness, explanation quality, and data diversity. Subsequently, we fine-tune the model on these well-curated training data as a cold start and further optimize it with rule-based reinforcement learning, using rewards for both prediction correctness and explanation quality. Results on 12 diverse tasks show that the 8B-parameter FaithLens outperforms advanced models such as GPT-5.2 and o3. Also, FaithLens can produce high-quality explanations, delivering a distinctive balance of trustworthiness, efficiency, and effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FaithLens：检测与解释忠实性幻觉
识别大语言模型输出是否包含忠实性幻觉对实际应用至关重要，例如检索增强生成与文本摘要。本文提出FaithLens——一种高效经济的忠实性幻觉检测模型，可同时提供二元预测及相应解释以增强可信度。我们首先通过先进大语言模型合成含解释的训练数据，并采用严格的数据过滤策略确保标签准确性、解释质量与数据多样性。随后基于这些高质量训练数据进行冷启动微调，并通过基于规则的强化学习进一步优化模型，其奖励机制同时考量预测准确性与解释质量。在12项多样化任务上的实验表明，80亿参数的FaithLens在性能上超越GPT-5.2及o3等先进模型，且能生成高质量解释，在可信度、效率与效能间实现卓越平衡。

TRN-R1-Zero: Text-rich Network Reasoning via LLMs with Reinforcement Learning Only
Authors: Yilun Liu, Ruihong Qiu, Zi Huang
First: 2026-04-21T04:24:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:24:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Zero-shot reasoning on text-rich networks (TRNs) remains a challenging frontier, as models must integrate textual semantics with relational structure without task-specific supervision. While graph neural networks rely on fixed label spaces and supervised objectives, recent large language model (LLM)-based approaches often overlook graph context or depend on distillation from larger models, limiting generalisation. We propose TRN-R1-Zero, a post-training framework for TRN reasoning trained solely via reinforcement learning. TRN-R1-Zero directly optimises base LLMs using a Neighbour-aware Group Relative Policy Optimisation objective that dynamically adjusts rewards based on a novel margin gain metric for the informativeness of neighbouring signals, effectively guiding the model toward relational reasoning. Unlike prior methods, TRN-R1-Zero requires no supervised fine-tuning or chain-of-thought data generated from large reasoning models. Extensive experiments across citation, hyperlink, social and co-purchase TRN benchmarks demonstrate the superiority and robustness of TRN-R1-Zero. Moreover, relying strictly on node-level training, TRN-R1-Zero achieves zero-shot inference on edge- and graph-level tasks, extending beyond cross-domain transfer. The codebase is publicly available at https://github.com/superallen13/TRN-R1-Zero.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TRN-R1-Zero：基于纯强化学习的大语言模型文本富网络推理方法
文本富网络的零样本推理仍是一个具有挑战性的前沿领域，因为模型必须在无任务特定监督的情况下整合文本语义与关系结构。图神经网络依赖固定标签空间和监督目标，而近期基于大语言模型的方法常忽略图上下文或依赖大模型蒸馏，限制了泛化能力。我们提出TRN-R1-Zero——一个完全通过强化学习训练的文本富网络推理后训练框架。该框架采用邻居感知分组相对策略优化目标直接优化基础大语言模型，该目标通过创新的边界增益指标动态调整邻居信号信息量的奖励，有效引导模型进行关系推理。与先前方法不同，TRN-R1-Zero无需监督微调或从大型推理模型生成的思维链数据。在引用、超链接、社交和共同购买等文本富网络基准上的大量实验证明了TRN-R1-Zero的优越性与鲁棒性。此外，通过严格依赖节点级训练，TRN-R1-Zero实现了边级和图级任务的零样本推理，其能力已超越跨领域迁移范畴。代码库已公开于https://github.com/superallen13/TRN-R1-Zero。

The proposed method, TRN-R1-Zero, is a post-training framework that uses reinforcement learning exclusively, optimizing base large language models with a Neighbour-aware Group Relative Policy Optimisation objective that dynamically adjusts rewards based on a margin gain metric to enhance relational reasoning, without requiring supervised fine-tuning or chain-of-thought data. Experimental results across citation, hyperlink, social, and co-purchase benchmarks show the framework's superiority and robustness, achieving zero-shot inference on edge- and graph-level tasks and extending to cross-domain transfer.

MRS: Multi-Resolution Skills for HRL Agents
Authors: Shashank Sharma, Janina Hoffmann, Vinay Namboodiri
First: 2025-05-27T16:38:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:20:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) decomposes the policy into a manager and a worker, enabling long-horizon planning but introducing a performance gap on tasks requiring agility. We identify a root cause: in subgoal-based HRL, the manager's goal representation is typically learned without constraints on reachability or temporal distance from the current state, preventing precise local subgoal selection. We further show that the optimal subgoal distance is both task- and state-dependent: nearby subgoals enable precise control but amplify prediction noise, while distant subgoals produce smoother motion at the cost of geometric precision. We propose Multi-Resolution Skills (MRS), which learns multiple goal-prediction modules each specialized to a fixed temporal horizon, with a jointly trained meta-controller that selects among them based on the current state. MRS consistently outperforms fixed-resolution baselines and significantly reduces the performance gap between HRL and non-HRL state-of-the-art on DeepMind Control Suite, Gym-Robotics, and long-horizon AntMaze tasks. [Project page: https://sites.google.com/view/multi-res-skills/home]
中文标题/摘要
标题：MRS：分层强化学习智能体的多分辨率技能
分层强化学习（HRL）将策略分解为管理器和执行器，虽能实现长时程规划，但在需要敏捷性的任务上存在性能差距。我们发现根本原因在于：基于子目标的HRL中，管理器的目标表征通常在学习时未考虑可达性或与当前状态的时间距离约束，导致无法精确选择局部子目标。研究进一步表明，最优子目标距离同时取决于任务和状态：邻近子目标可实现精确控制但会放大预测噪声，而远端子目标能以几何精度为代价生成更平滑的运动。我们提出多分辨率技能（MRS），该方法学习多个专门针对固定时间跨度的目标预测模块，并通过联合训练的元控制器根据当前状态进行选择。在DeepMind Control Suite、Gym-Robotics和长时程AntMaze任务中，MRS始终优于固定分辨率基线，并显著缩小了HRL与非HRL前沿方法之间的性能差距。[项目页面：https://sites.google.com/view/multi-res-skills/home]
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a performance gap in hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) where subgoal-based agents struggle with agile tasks due to unconstrained goal representations that lack reachability and temporal distance considerations, leading to imprecise local subgoal selection. The authors propose Multi-Resolution Skills (MRS), a method that learns multiple goal-prediction modules each specialized for a fixed temporal horizon, coupled with a meta-controller that dynamically selects among them based on the current state to balance control precision and motion smoothness. Experimental results on DeepMind Control Suite, Gym-Robotics, and AntMaze tasks show that MRS consistently outperforms fixed-resolution baselines and significantly narrows the performance gap between HRL and non-HRL state-of-the-art approaches.
本文针对分层强化学习（HRL）中基于子目标的方法在敏捷任务上存在的性能差距，指出其根源在于管理器的目标表示通常缺乏对可达性和时间距离的约束，导致局部子目标选择不精确。作者提出了多分辨率技能（MRS）方法，该方法学习多个专注于固定时间范围的子目标预测模块，并通过联合训练的元控制器根据当前状态动态选择模块，以在控制精度和运动平滑性之间取得平衡。在DeepMind Control Suite、Gym-Robotics和AntMaze任务上的实验结果表明，MRS一致优于固定分辨率基线，并显著缩小了HRL与非HRL先进方法之间的性能差距。
Reinforcement Learning Improves LLM Accuracy and Reasoning in Disease Classification from Radiology Reports
Authors: Yishu Wei, Yi Lin, Adam Flanders, George Shih, Yifan Peng
First: 2026-04-21T04:09:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T04:09:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate disease classification from radiology reports is essential for many applications. While supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of lightweight LLMs improves accuracy, it can degrade reasoning. We propose a two-stage approach: SFT on disease labels followed by Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to refine predictions by optimizing accuracy and format without reasoning supervision. Across three radiologist-annotated datasets, SFT outperformed baselines and GRPO further improved classification and enhanced reasoning recall and comprehensiveness.

从放射学报告中准确分类疾病对许多应用至关重要。虽然轻量化大语言模型的监督微调能提升准确性，但可能削弱推理能力。我们提出一种两阶段方法：先基于疾病标签进行监督微调，再通过群体相对策略优化在无推理监督的情况下优化准确性与格式以精炼预测。在三个放射科医师标注的数据集上，监督微调优于基线模型，而群体相对策略优化进一步提升了分类性能，并增强了推理的召回率与全面性。

This study addresses the challenge of maintaining reasoning capabilities in lightweight large language models (LLMs) when they are fine-tuned for accurate disease classification from radiology reports. The authors propose a two-stage method: first performing supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on disease labels, followed by applying Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to refine predictions by jointly optimizing for accuracy and output format, all without explicit reasoning supervision. Experimental results on three radiologist-annotated datasets show that SFT outperformed baseline models, and the subsequent GRPO stage further improved classification performance while also enhancing the models' reasoning recall and comprehensiveness.

QTMRL: An Agent for Quantitative Trading Decision-Making Based on Multi-Indicator Guided Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingfeng Pan, Jiahao Chen
First: 2025-08-28T06:37:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:38:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In the highly volatile and uncertain global financial markets, traditional quantitative trading models relying on statistical modeling or empirical rules often fail to adapt to dynamic market changes and black swan events due to rigid assumptions and limited generalization. To address these issues, this paper proposes QTMRL (Quantitative Trading Multi-Indicator Reinforcement Learning), an intelligent trading agent combining multi-dimensional technical indicators with reinforcement learning (RL) for adaptive and stable portfolio management. We first construct a comprehensive multi-indicator dataset using 23 years of S&P 500 daily OHLCV data (2000-2022) for 16 representative stocks across 5 sectors, enriching raw data with trend, volatility, and momentum indicators to capture holistic market dynamics. Then we design a lightweight RL framework based on the Advantage Actor-Critic (A2C) algorithm, including data processing, A2C algorithm, and trading agent modules to support policy learning and actionable trading decisions. Extensive experiments compare QTMRL with 9 baselines (e.g., ARIMA, LSTM, moving average strategies) across diverse market regimes, verifying its superiority in profitability, risk adjustment, and downside risk control. The code of QTMRL is publicly available at https://github.com/ChenJiahaoJNU/QTMRL.git
中文标题/摘要

The method constructs a comprehensive dataset using 23 years of S&P 500 data enriched with trend, volatility, and momentum indicators, and employs a lightweight Advantage Actor-Critic (A2C) framework to learn trading policies. Experimental results demonstrate that QTMRL outperforms nine baselines, including ARIMA and LSTM, across various market conditions in terms of profitability, risk-adjusted returns, and downside risk control.
针对传统量化交易模型在动态不确定金融市场中适应性不足的问题，本文提出QTMRL智能交易代理，将多维技术指标与强化学习相结合以实现自适应投资组合管理。该方法基于23年标普500数据构建包含趋势、波动和动量指标的综合数据集，并采用轻量级优势演员-评论家（A2C）框架进行策略学习。实验结果表明，在不同市场环境下，QTMRL在盈利能力、风险调整收益和下行风险控制方面均优于ARIMA、LSTM等九种基线模型。
Intentional Updates for Streaming Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Arsalan Sharifnassab, Mohamed Elsayed, Kris De Asis, A. Rupam Mahmood, Richard S. Sutton
First: 2026-04-21T03:33:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:33:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In gradient-based learning, a step size chosen in parameter units does not produce a predictable per-step change in function output. This often leads to instability in the streaming setting (i.e., batch size=1), where stochasticity is not averaged out and update magnitudes can momentarily become arbitrarily big or small. Instead, we propose intentional updates: first specify the intended outcome of an update and then solve for the step size that approximately achieves it. This strategy has precedent in online supervised linear regression via Normalized Least Mean Squares algorithm, which selects a step size to yield a specified change in the function output proportional to the current error. We extend this principle to streaming deep reinforcement learning by defining appropriate intended outcomes: Intentional TD aims for a fixed fractional reduction of the TD error, and Intentional Policy Gradient aims for a bounded per-step change in the policy, limiting local KL divergence. We propose practical algorithms combining eligibility traces and diagonal scaling. Empirically, these methods yield state-of-the-art streaming performance, frequently performing on par with batch and replay-buffer approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：流式强化学习中的意图性更新
在基于梯度的学习中，以参数单位选择的步长不会在函数输出中产生可预测的每步变化。这在流式设置（即批大小=1）中常导致不稳定性，其中随机性未被平均化，更新幅度可能瞬时变得任意大或小。为此，我们提出意图性更新：首先明确更新的预期目标，然后求解近似实现该目标的步长。该策略在在线监督线性回归中已有先例，如归一化最小均方算法通过选择步长使函数输出产生与当前误差成比例的指定变化。我们将此原理扩展至流式深度强化学习，定义适当的预期目标：意图性时序差分旨在实现时序差分误差的固定比例缩减，意图性策略梯度则旨在限制策略的每步变化，约束局部KL散度。我们提出了结合资格迹与对角缩放的实用算法。实验表明，这些方法实现了先进的流式性能，常能与批处理和回放缓冲方法相媲美。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses instability in streaming reinforcement learning, where traditional gradient-based methods with fixed step sizes can lead to unpredictable and often divergent updates due to high stochasticity. To mitigate this, the authors propose intentional updates, a method that first defines a desired outcome for each update—such as a fixed fractional reduction in temporal-difference error or a bounded change in policy—and then solves for the step size to achieve it, extending principles from online supervised learning. Experimental results show that the proposed algorithms, which incorporate eligibility traces and diagonal scaling, achieve state-of-the-art performance in streaming settings, often matching the effectiveness of batch and replay-buffer approaches.
本文针对流式强化学习中的不稳定性问题展开研究，传统基于梯度的学习方法因固定步长在高度随机性下易导致更新不可预测甚至发散。为解决此问题，作者提出意图性更新方法，该方法首先定义每次更新的预期目标——例如固定比例减少时序差分误差或限制策略的局部KL散度变化——然后求解实现该目标的步长，扩展了在线监督学习的原理。实验结果表明，结合资格迹和对角缩放的所提算法在流式设置中取得了先进的性能，常能与批处理和回放缓冲方法相媲美。
Benchmarking Swarm Optimization Algorithms for Parameter Initialization in the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm
Authors: Shashank Sanjay Bhat, Peiyong Wang, Udaya Parampalli
First: 2025-06-07T13:14:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:23:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) is a prominent variational algorithm for solving combinatorial optimization problems such as the Max Cut problem. A key challenge in QAOA is the efficient identification of variational parameters (γ, \{beta}) that yield high-quality solutions. In this work, we investigate swarm optimization methods as robust strategies for exploring the QAOA parameter space. We evaluate Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO), Fully Informed Particle Swarm Optimization (FIPSO), Quantum Particle Swarm Optimization (QPSO), and an Adam-assisted FIPSO variant on weighted MaxCut instances across multiple system sizes, circuit depths, and noise regimes, including shot noise. Our results show that these methods achieve lower approximation gaps and more stable convergence compared to standard optimizers such as Adam, COBYLA, and SPSA. In particular, we observe that swarm methods maintain superior performance under noisy and shot limited conditions. These findings suggest that population based search is effective for navigating the complex QAOA landscape and is a promising approach for parameter optimization in near-term quantum algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量子近似优化算法参数初始化的群体优化算法基准测试
量子近似优化算法（QAOA）是解决组合优化问题（如最大割问题）的重要变分算法。QAOA的关键挑战在于高效识别能产生高质量解的变分参数（γ, β）。本研究探讨了群体优化方法作为探索QAOA参数空间的稳健策略。我们在加权最大割实例上，针对多种系统规模、电路深度和噪声机制（包括散粒噪声），评估了粒子群优化（PSO）、全信息粒子群优化（FIPSO）、量子粒子群优化（QPSO）以及Adam辅助的FIPSO变体。结果表明，与Adam、COBYLA和SPSA等标准优化器相比，这些方法实现了更低的近似误差和更稳定的收敛性。特别值得注意的是，群体优化方法在噪声和散粒受限条件下仍保持优越性能。这些发现表明，基于群体的搜索能有效探索复杂的QAOA参数空间，是近期量子算法参数优化的有效途径。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the challenge of efficiently finding high-quality variational parameters in the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) for combinatorial problems like MaxCut. The method involves benchmarking several swarm optimization algorithms—including Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO), Fully Informed PSO (FIPSO), Quantum PSO (QPSO), and an Adam-assisted FIPSO variant—across various weighted MaxCut instances, system sizes, circuit depths, and noise conditions. The main experimental results demonstrate that these swarm methods achieve lower approximation gaps and more stable convergence than standard optimizers like Adam, COBYLA, and SPSA, with particularly robust performance under noisy and shot-limited settings, indicating that population-based search is effective for navigating the complex QAOA parameter landscape.
本研究的动机是解决量子近似优化算法（QAOA）在解决如最大割等组合优化问题时，高效寻找高质量变分参数的挑战。方法上，研究对多种群优化算法进行了基准测试，包括粒子群优化（PSO）、完全信息粒子群优化（FIPSO）、量子粒子群优化（QPSO）以及一种Adam辅助的FIPSO变体，测试覆盖了不同权重的最大割实例、系统规模、电路深度和噪声条件。主要实验结果表明，这些群优化方法相比Adam、COBYLA和SPSA等标准优化器，获得了更低的近似误差和更稳定的收敛性，尤其在噪声和有限测量次数条件下仍保持优越性能，这表明基于种群的搜索能有效探索复杂的QAOA参数空间。
Policy Gradient Primal-Dual Method for Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback
Authors: Qiang Liu, Adrienne Kline, Ermin Wei
First: 2026-04-21T03:20:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:20:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (Safe RLHF) has recently achieved empirical success in developing helpful and harmless large language models by decoupling human preferences regarding helpfulness and harmlessness. Existing approaches typically rely on fitting fixed horizon reward models from human feedback and have only been validated empirically. In this paper, we formulate safe RLHF as an infinite horizon discounted Con- strained Markov Decision Process (CMDP), since humans may interact with the model over a continuing sequence of interactions rather than within a single finite episode. We propose two Safe RLHF algorithms that do not require reward model fitting and, in contrast to prior work assuming fixed-length trajectories, support flexible trajectory lengths for training. Both algo- rithms are based on the primal-dual method and achieve global convergence guarantees with polynomial rates in terms of policy gradient iterations, trajectory sample lengths, and human preference queries. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to study infinite horizon discounted CMDP under human feedback and establish global, non-asymptotic convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于策略梯度的原对偶方法用于人类反馈的安全强化学习
人类反馈的安全强化学习（Safe RLHF）近期通过解耦人类对有用性和无害性的偏好，在开发有益且无害的大型语言模型方面取得了实证成功。现有方法通常依赖于从人类反馈中拟合固定时间范围的奖励模型，且仅经过实证验证。本文提出将安全RLHF建模为无限时间范围折扣约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP），因为人类可能与模型进行持续交互而非单一有限回合。我们提出了两种无需奖励模型拟合的安全RLHF算法，与先前假设固定长度轨迹的研究不同，这些算法支持灵活的训练轨迹长度。两种算法均基于原对偶方法，并在策略梯度迭代、轨迹样本长度和人类偏好查询方面实现了具有多项式速率的全局收敛保证。据我们所知，这是首个研究人类反馈下无限时间范围折扣CMDP并建立全局非渐近收敛性的工作。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to develop safe and helpful large language models through human feedback, this paper formulates Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (Safe RLHF) as an infinite horizon discounted Constrained Markov Decision Process to account for continuing human interactions. The method introduces two primal-dual policy gradient algorithms that eliminate the need for fitting fixed reward models and support flexible trajectory lengths during training. The main experimental results demonstrate that these algorithms achieve global convergence with polynomial rates in policy gradient iterations, sample lengths, and human preference queries, providing the first non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for infinite horizon discounted CMDPs under human feedback.
本文旨在通过人类反馈开发安全且有益的大型语言模型，其动机是将安全强化学习人类反馈问题建模为无限时域折扣约束马尔可夫决策过程，以适应持续的人类交互场景。方法上提出了两种基于原始对偶策略梯度的算法，无需拟合固定奖励模型，并支持训练中轨迹长度的灵活性。主要实验结果证明，这些算法在策略梯度迭代、样本长度和人类偏好查询方面实现了多项式速率的全局收敛，为人类反馈下的无限时域折扣约束马尔可夫决策过程首次建立了非渐近的收敛性保证。
LEPO: Latent Reasoning Policy Optimization for Large Language Models
Authors: Yuyan Zhou, Jiarui Yu, Hande Dong, Zhezheng Hao, Hong Wang, Jianqing Zhang, Qiang Lin
First: 2026-04-20T07:05:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:14:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recently, latent reasoning has been introduced into large language models (LLMs) to leverage rich information within a continuous space. However, without stochastic sampling, these methods inevitably collapse to deterministic inference, failing to discover diverse reasoning paths. To bridge the gap, we inject controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, restoring LLMs' exploratory capacity and enhancing their compatibility with Reinforcement Learning (RL). Building on this, we propose \textbf{\underline{L}}atent R\textbf{\underline{e}}asoning \textbf{\underline{P}}olicy \textbf{\underline{O}}ptimization~(\textbf{LEPO}), a novel framework that applies RL directly to continuous latent representations. Specifically, in rollout stage, LEPO maintains stochasticity to enable diverse trajectory sampling, while in optimization stage, LEPO constructs a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens. Extensive experiments show that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for discrete and latent reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LEPO：面向大语言模型的潜在推理策略优化
近期，潜在推理被引入大语言模型（LLMs）以利用连续空间中的丰富信息。然而，由于缺乏随机采样，这些方法不可避免地退化为确定性推理，无法发现多样化的推理路径。为弥补这一不足，我们通过Gumbel-Softmax向潜在推理注入可控随机性，恢复LLMs的探索能力并增强其与强化学习（RL）的兼容性。在此基础上，我们提出\textbf{\underline{L}}atent R\textbf{\underline{e}}asoning \textbf{\underline{P}}olicy \textbf{\underline{O}}ptimization~(\textbf{LEPO})——一种直接将RL应用于连续潜在表征的新框架。具体而言，在推演阶段，LEPO保持随机性以实现多样化轨迹采样；在优化阶段，LEPO为潜在表征和离散标记构建统一的梯度估计。大量实验表明，LEPO在离散与潜在推理任务上显著优于现有RL方法。

The paper introduces LEPO, a framework designed to enhance large language models (LLMs) by addressing the deterministic collapse in latent reasoning methods, which limits the discovery of diverse reasoning paths. The method injects controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, enabling exploratory capacity and compatibility with Reinforcement Learning (RL), and applies RL directly to continuous latent representations through a novel policy optimization approach that maintains stochasticity during rollouts and provides unified gradient estimation. Experimental results demonstrate that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for both discrete and latent reasoning tasks.
本文提出了LEPO框架，旨在解决大语言模型中潜在推理方法因确定性推断而无法探索多样化推理路径的问题。该方法通过Gumbel-Softmax向潜在推理注入可控随机性，以恢复模型的探索能力并增强其与强化学习的兼容性，进而将强化学习直接应用于连续潜在表示，在轨迹采样阶段保持随机性，在优化阶段构建统一梯度估计。实验结果表明，LEPO在离散和潜在推理任务上显著优于现有的强化学习方法。
UDM-GRPO: Stable and Efficient Group Relative Policy Optimization for Uniform Discrete Diffusion Models
Authors: Jiaqi Wang, Haoge Deng, Ting Pan, Yang Liu, Chengyuan Wang, Fan Zhang, Yonggang Qi, Xinlong Wang
First: 2026-04-20T17:16:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T03:05:09+00:00
Comments: Code is available at https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Uniform Discrete Diffusion Model (UDM) has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for discrete generative modeling; however, its integration with reinforcement learning remains largely unexplored. We observe that naively applying GRPO to UDM leads to training instability and marginal performance gains. To address this, we propose UDM-GRPO, the first framework to integrate UDM with RL. Our method is guided by two key insights: (i) treating the final clean sample as the action provides more accurate and stable optimization signals; and (ii) reconstructing trajectories via the diffusion forward process better aligns probability paths with the pretraining distribution. Additionally, we introduce two strategies, Reduced-Step and CFG-Free, to further improve training efficiency. UDM-GRPO significantly improves base model performance across multiple T2I tasks. Notably, GenEval accuracy improves from $69\%$ to $96\%$ and PickScore increases from $20.46$ to $23.81$, achieving state-of-the-art performance in both continuous and discrete settings. On the OCR benchmark, accuracy rises from $8\%$ to $57\%$, further validating the generalization ability of our method. Code is available at https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UDM-GRPO：面向均匀离散扩散模型的稳定高效群体相对策略优化
均匀离散扩散模型（UDM）近期成为离散生成建模的重要范式，但其与强化学习的结合尚未得到充分探索。研究发现，直接将GRPO应用于UDM会导致训练不稳定且性能提升有限。为此，我们提出首个将UDM与强化学习融合的框架UDM-GRPO。该方法基于两个关键洞见：（1）将最终纯净样本作为动作能提供更精确稳定的优化信号；（2）通过扩散前向过程重构轨迹可使概率路径与预训练分布更好对齐。此外，我们引入“降阶采样”与“免分类器引导”策略以提升训练效率。UDM-GRPO在多项文生图任务中显著提升基础模型性能：GenEval准确率从69%提升至96%，PickScore从20.46提升至23.81，在连续与离散设定下均达到最优性能。在OCR基准测试中，准确率从8%提升至57%，进一步验证了方法的泛化能力。代码已开源：https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of integrating Uniform Discrete Diffusion Models (UDM) with reinforcement learning, as naive application of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) leads to instability and limited gains. The proposed UDM-GRPO framework introduces two key methodological insights: treating the final clean sample as the action for stable optimization signals and reconstructing trajectories via the diffusion forward process to align with pretraining distributions, supplemented by Reduced-Step and CFG-Free strategies for efficiency. Experimental results demonstrate significant performance improvements, with GenEval accuracy rising from 69% to 96%, PickScore increasing from 20.46 to 23.81, and OCR benchmark accuracy jumping from 8% to 57%, achieving state-of-the-art results in both continuous and discrete settings.
本文针对均匀离散扩散模型与强化学习结合时，直接应用组相对策略优化会导致训练不稳定和性能提升有限的问题，提出了UDM-GRPO框架。该方法基于两个核心思路：将最终干净样本作为动作以提供更稳定的优化信号，以及通过扩散前向过程重构轨迹以更好地对齐预训练分布，并辅以缩减步数和免分类器引导策略来提升效率。实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了基础模型性能，在多项文本到图像任务中，GenEval准确率从69%提高到96%，PickScore从20.46提升至23.81，OCR基准准确率从8%跃升至57%，在连续和离散设置下均达到了最先进的性能水平。
Guiding Distribution Matching Distillation with Gradient-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Linwei Dong, Ruoyu Guo, Ge Bai, Zehuan Yuan, Yawei Luo, Changqing Zou
First: 2026-04-21T02:57:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T02:57:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion distillation, exemplified by Distribution Matching Distillation (DMD), has shown great promise in few-step generation but often sacrifices quality for sampling speed. While integrating Reinforcement Learning (RL) into distillation offers potential, a naive fusion of these two objectives relies on suboptimal raw sample evaluation. This sample-based scoring creates inherent conflicts with the distillation trajectory and produces unreliable rewards due to the noisy nature of early-stage generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose GDMD, a novel framework that redefines the reward mechanism by prioritizing distillation gradients over raw pixel outputs as the primary signal for optimization. By reinterpreting the DMD gradients as implicit target tensors, our framework enables existing reward models to directly evaluate the quality of distillation updates. This gradient-level guidance functions as an adaptive weighting that synchronizes the RL policy with the distillation objective, effectively neutralizing optimization divergence. Empirical results show that GDMD sets a new SOTA for few-step generation. Specifically, our 4-step models outperform the quality of their multi-step teacher and substantially exceed previous DMDR results in GenEval and human-preference metrics, exhibiting strong scalability potential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于梯度强化学习的分布匹配蒸馏引导方法
以分布匹配蒸馏为代表的扩散蒸馏方法在少步生成中展现出巨大潜力，但常为采样速度牺牲生成质量。虽然将强化学习融入蒸馏具有改进潜力，但两种目标的简单融合依赖于次优的原始样本评估。这种基于样本的评分机制与蒸馏轨迹存在固有冲突，且早期生成阶段的噪声特性会导致奖励信号不可靠。为突破这些局限，我们提出GDMD框架，通过将蒸馏梯度（而非原始像素输出）作为主要优化信号，重构奖励机制。通过将DMD梯度重新解释为隐式目标张量，我们的框架使现有奖励模型能直接评估蒸馏更新的质量。这种梯度级引导作为自适应权重，使强化学习策略与蒸馏目标同步，有效消除优化分歧。实验表明GDMD在少步生成任务上达到最新最优水平：我们的4步模型在生成质量上超越多步教师模型，并在GenEval指标和人工偏好评估中显著超越先前DMDR结果，展现出强大的扩展潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the quality degradation in few-step diffusion distillation, such as Distribution Matching Distillation (DMD), when combined with Reinforcement Learning (RL), where sample-based rewards conflict with the distillation process. The proposed method, GDMD, introduces a novel framework that uses distillation gradients as implicit target tensors for reward models, allowing direct evaluation of update quality and aligning the RL policy with the distillation objective to prevent optimization divergence. Experimental results demonstrate that GDMD achieves state-of-the-art performance in few-step generation, with 4-step models surpassing their multi-step teachers and outperforming prior DMDR results on GenEval and human-preference metrics, showing strong scalability.
本文针对少步扩散蒸馏（如分布匹配蒸馏DMD）与强化学习结合时因样本奖励与蒸馏轨迹冲突导致的质量下降问题，提出了一种新框架GDMD。该方法将蒸馏梯度重新解释为隐式目标张量，使奖励模型能直接评估更新质量，从而同步强化学习策略与蒸馏目标，有效消除优化分歧。实验结果表明，GDMD在少步生成任务中取得了最先进的性能，其4步模型的质量超越了多步教师模型，并在GenEval和人类偏好指标上显著优于先前的DMDR结果，展现出强大的可扩展潜力。
SAVOIR: Learning Social Savoir-Faire via Shapley-based Reward Attribution
Authors: Xiachong Feng, Yi Jiang, Xiaocheng Feng, Deyi Yin, Libo Qin, Yangfan Ye, Lei Huang, Weitao Ma, Yuxuan Gu, Chonghan Qin, Bing Qin, Lingpeng Kong
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-21T02:08:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T02:08:25+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Social intelligence, the ability to navigate complex interpersonal interactions, presents a fundamental challenge for language agents. Training such agents via reinforcement learning requires solving the credit assignment problem: determining how individual utterances contribute to multi-turn dialogue outcomes. Existing approaches directly employ language models to distribute episode-level rewards, yielding attributions that are retrospective and lack theoretical grounding. We propose SAVOIR (ShApley Value fOr SocIal RL), a novel principled framework grounded in cooperative game theory. Our approach combines two complementary principles: expected utility shifts evaluation from retrospective attribution to prospective valuation, capturing an utterance's strategic potential for enabling favorable future trajectories; Shapley values ensure fair credit distribution with axiomatic guarantees of efficiency, symmetry, and marginality. Experiments on the SOTOPIA benchmark demonstrate that SAVOIR achieves new state-of-the-art performance across all evaluation settings, with our 7B model matching or exceeding proprietary models including GPT-4o and Claude-3.5-Sonnet. Notably, even large reasoning models consistently underperform, suggesting social intelligence requires qualitatively different capabilities than analytical reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAVOIR：基于沙普利值奖励归因的社会处世能力学习
社交智能——驾驭复杂人际互动的能力——是语言智能体面临的根本挑战。通过强化学习训练此类智能体需解决信用分配问题：确定个体话语如何影响多轮对话结果。现有方法直接使用语言模型分配回合级奖励，其归因方式具有回溯性且缺乏理论依据。我们提出SAVOIR（基于沙普利值的社会强化学习框架），这是一个植根于合作博弈论的新型原则性框架。该方法融合两个互补原则：期望效用将评估从回溯归因转向前瞻估值，捕捉话语促成有利未来轨迹的战略潜力；沙普利值通过效率性、对称性、边际性的公理保证实现公平信用分配。在SOTOPIA基准测试中，SAVOIR在所有评估设定下均达到最新最优性能，其70亿参数模型匹配或超越了包括GPT-4o与Claude-3.5-Sonnet在内的专有模型。值得注意的是，即使大型推理模型也持续表现不佳，表明社交智能需要与分析推理截然不同的能力特质。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of training socially intelligent language agents, where existing methods for credit assignment in multi-turn dialogues are retrospective and lack theoretical grounding, this paper introduces SAVOIR, a principled framework based on cooperative game theory. The method combines expected utility for prospective valuation of an utterance's strategic potential with Shapley values to ensure fair credit distribution with axiomatic guarantees. Experimental results on the SOTOPIA benchmark show that SAVOIR achieves state-of-the-art performance, with a 7B model matching or exceeding proprietary models like GPT-4o and Claude-3.5-Sonnet, while also demonstrating that large reasoning models underperform, indicating social intelligence requires distinct capabilities.
本文针对训练具有社会智能的语言智能体所面临的挑战而提出，现有方法在多轮对话的信用分配上具有回顾性且缺乏理论依据。为此，论文引入了SAVOIR这一基于合作博弈论的原理性框架，其方法结合了期望效用（用于前瞻性评估话语的战略潜力）和沙普利值（以确保具有公理保证的公平信用分配）。在SOTOPIA基准上的实验结果表明，SAVOIR取得了最先进的性能，其70亿参数模型匹配甚至超越了GPT-4o和Claude-3.5-Sonnet等专有模型，同时发现大型推理模型表现不佳，表明社会智能需要与解析推理不同的能力。
Low-Rank Adaptation for Critic Learning in Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuan Zhuang, Yuexin Bian, Sihong He, Jie Feng, Qing Su, Songyang Han, Jonathan Petit, Shihao Ji, Yuanyuan Shi, Fei Miao
First: 2026-04-21T01:59:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T01:59:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling critic capacity is a promising direction for enhancing off-policy reinforcement learning (RL). However, larger critics are prone to overfitting and unstable in replay-buffer-based bootstrap training. This paper leverages Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) as a structural-sparsity regularizer for off-policy critics. Our approach freezes randomly initialized base matrices and solely optimizes low-rank adapters, thereby constraining critic updates to a low-dimensional subspace. Built on top of SimbaV2, we further develop a LoRA formulation, compatible with SimbaV2, that preserves its hyperspherical normalization geometry under frozen-backbone training. We evaluate our method with SAC and FastTD3 on DeepMind Control locomotion and IsaacLab robotics benchmarks. LoRA consistently achieves lower critic loss during training and stronger policy performance. Extensive experiments demonstrate that adaptive low-rank updates provide a simple, scalable, and effective structural regularization for critic learning in off-policy RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线策略强化学习中基于低秩适配的评论家学习
扩展评论家容量是提升离线策略强化学习性能的有效途径，但更大的评论家网络容易在基于经验回放池的自举训练中出现过拟合与不稳定问题。本文提出将低秩适配作为离线策略评论家的结构稀疏正则化方法：冻结随机初始化的基础矩阵，仅优化低秩适配器，从而将评论家更新约束在低维子空间。基于SimbaV2框架，我们进一步设计了兼容其几何特性的LoRA实现方案，在冻结主干网络训练时保持超球面归一化几何结构。通过在DeepMind Control运动控制与IsaacLab机器人基准测试中结合SAC和FastTD3算法进行评估，LoRA在训练过程中始终获得更低的评论家损失与更强的策略性能。大量实验表明，自适应低秩更新为离线强化学习的评论家训练提供了一种简洁、可扩展且高效的结构正则化方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of scaling critic capacity in off-policy reinforcement learning, where larger critics often suffer from overfitting and instability during bootstrap training. The method leverages Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) as a structural-sparsity regularizer by freezing randomly initialized base matrices and optimizing only low-rank adapters, thus constraining critic updates to a low-dimensional subspace; it further develops a LoRA formulation compatible with SimbaV2 to preserve its hyperspherical normalization geometry. Experimental results on DeepMind Control locomotion and IsaacLab robotics benchmarks with SAC and FastTD3 show that LoRA consistently achieves lower critic loss during training and stronger policy performance, demonstrating its effectiveness as a simple, scalable regularization technique.
本文针对离线策略强化学习中批评家网络规模扩大时易过拟合和训练不稳定的问题，提出使用低秩适应（LoRA）作为结构稀疏正则化方法。该方法冻结随机初始化的基础矩阵，仅优化低秩适配器，从而将批评家更新限制在低维子空间；并开发了与SimbaV2兼容的LoRA形式，以在冻结主干训练时保持其超球面归一化几何特性。在DeepMind Control运动控制和IsaacLab机器人基准测试中，结合SAC和FastTD3算法的实验结果表明，LoRA在训练中持续获得更低的批评家损失和更强的策略性能，验证了其作为一种简单、可扩展的正则化方法的有效性。
Self-Improving Tabular Language Models via Iterative Group Alignment
Authors: Yunbo Long, Tejumade Afonja, Alexandra Brintrup, Mario Fritz
First: 2026-04-21T01:29:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T01:29:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While language models have been adapted for tabular data generation, two fundamental limitations remain: (1) static fine-tuning produces models that cannot learn from their own generated samples and adapt to self-correct, and (2) autoregressive objectives preserve local token coherence but neglect global statistical properties, degrading tabular quality. Reinforcement learning offers a potential solution but requires designing reward functions that balance competing objectives -- impractical for tabular data. To fill the gap, we introduce TabGRAA (Tabular Group-Relative Advantage Alignment), the first self-improving framework for tabular data generation via automated feedback. At each iteration, TabGRAA uses an \emph{automated quality signal} -- such as a two-sample distinguishability classifier or a distance-based reward -- to partition newly generated samples into high- and low-quality groups, then optimizes a group-relative advantage objective that reinforces realistic patterns while penalizing artifacts. The specific signal is a modular choice rather than a fixed component of the framework. This establishes a virtuous feedback cycle, where the quality signal is re-computed against newly \emph{generated synthetic} samples at each round; the language model is only fine-tuned on these self-generated signals, so no additional real record is exposed during alignment, mitigating data-leakage risk beyond the initial supervised fine-tuning. Experiments show TabGRAA outperforms existing methods in fidelity, utility, and privacy, while matching or exceeding diffusion-based synthesizers, advancing tabular synthesis from static statistical replication to dynamic, self-improving generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过迭代分组对齐实现表格语言模型的自改进
尽管语言模型已应用于表格数据生成，仍存在两个根本性局限：(1)静态微调产生的模型无法从自身生成样本中学习并实现自适应修正；(2)自回归目标虽保持局部标记连贯性，却忽略全局统计特性，导致表格质量下降。强化学习虽提供潜在解决方案，但需设计平衡多目标的奖励函数——这对表格数据并不实用。为填补这一空白，我们提出TabGRAA（表格分组相对优势对齐框架），这是首个通过自动化反馈实现表格数据生成的自改进框架。每轮迭代中，TabGRAA利用自动化质量信号（如双样本可区分性分类器或基于距离的奖励）将新生成样本划分为高/低质量组，随后优化分组相对优势目标以强化真实模式并抑制伪影。该质量信号是模块化选项而非框架固定组件。由此建立良性反馈循环：每轮针对新生成的合成样本重新计算质量信号；语言模型仅基于这些自生成信号进行微调，确保在对齐阶段无需暴露额外真实记录，从而将数据泄露风险控制在初始监督微调范围内。实验表明TabGRAA在保真度、实用性与隐私性上均超越现有方法，性能匹配或优于基于扩散的合成器，推动表格合成从静态统计复制迈向动态自改进生成。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of static fine-tuning and autoregressive objectives in tabular data generation, which fail to enable self-correction and neglect global statistical properties, this paper introduces TabGRAA, a self-improving framework that uses automated quality signals to partition generated samples into high- and low-quality groups and optimizes a group-relative advantage objective. The method establishes an iterative feedback cycle where the model learns from its own synthetic samples without exposing additional real data, mitigating privacy risks. Experimental results demonstrate that TabGRAA outperforms existing methods in fidelity, utility, and privacy, matching or exceeding diffusion-based synthesizers and advancing tabular synthesis toward dynamic self-improvement.
针对表格数据生成中静态微调无法自我修正、自回归目标忽略全局统计特性的问题，本文提出了TabGRAA框架，通过自动化质量信号将生成样本划分为高、低质量组，并优化组间相对优势目标，实现自我改进。该方法建立了迭代反馈循环，模型仅基于自身生成的合成样本进行微调，无需额外真实数据，降低了隐私泄露风险。实验结果表明，TabGRAA在保真度、实用性和隐私性上优于现有方法，性能匹配或超越基于扩散的合成器，推动了表格合成从静态统计复制向动态自我改进的转变。
Reasoning Structure Matters for Safety Alignment of Reasoning Models
Authors: Yeonjun In, Wonjoong Kim, Sangwu Park, Chanyoung Park
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-21T00:50:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T00:50:13+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large reasoning models (LRMs) achieve strong performance on complex reasoning tasks but often generate harmful responses to malicious user queries. This paper investigates the underlying cause of these safety risks and shows that the issue lies in the reasoning structure itself. Based on this insight, we claim that effective safety alignment can be achieved by altering the reasoning structure. We propose AltTrain, a simple yet effective post training method that explicitly alters the reasoning structure of LRMs. AltTrain is both practical and generalizable, requiring no complex reinforcement learning (RL) training or reward design, only supervised finetuning (SFT) with a lightweight 1K training examples. Experiments across LRM backbones and model sizes demonstrate strong safety alignment, along with robust generalization across reasoning, QA, summarization, and multilingual setting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理结构对推理模型安全对齐的重要性
大型推理模型（LRMs）在复杂推理任务上表现优异，但常对恶意用户查询生成有害回应。本文探究了这些安全风险的根本原因，指出问题源于推理结构本身。基于这一发现，我们认为通过改变推理结构可实现有效的安全对齐。我们提出AltTrain——一种简单高效的后训练方法，能显式改变LRMs的推理结构。该方法兼具实用性与泛化性，无需复杂的强化学习（RL）训练或奖励设计，仅需使用轻量化的1K训练样本进行监督微调（SFT）。跨LRM骨干网络与模型规模的实验表明，该方法实现了强大的安全对齐能力，并在推理、问答、摘要及多语言场景中展现出稳健的泛化性能。

Fine-Tuning Small Reasoning Models for Quantum Field Theory
Authors: Nathaniel S. Woodward, Zhiqi Gao, Yurii Kvasiuk, Kendrick M. Smith, Frederic Sala, Moritz Münchmeyer
First: 2026-04-21T00:21:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-21T00:21:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the growing application of Large Language Models (LLMs) to theoretical physics, there is little academic exploration into how domain-specific physics reasoning ability develops while training these models. To investigate this, we perform the first academic fine-tuning study of small (7B-parameter) reasoning models dedicated specifically to theoretical physics. Because open-source verifiable training data required to train such capabilities is scarce, we developed a robust data generation pipeline that can both create synthetic problems and make existing human-authored problems suitable for model training. Selecting Quantum Field Theory (QFT) as our primary domain, we generated over 2,500 synthetic problems alongside a curated collection of human-adapted problems sourced from arXiv and standard pedagogical resources. We conduct both Reinforcement Learning (RL) and Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) experiments, benchmarking performance gains as well as generalization to other physics domains. We perform an extensive analysis of model chains-of-though before and after fine-tuning, to understand how reasoning errors evolve during RL and SFT. Finally, we publicly release our data pipeline, verifiable QFT training data, and $\sim$200M tokens of QFT reasoning traces.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向量子场论的小型推理模型微调研究

From Particles to Perils: SVGD-Based Hazardous Scenario Generation for Autonomous Driving Systems Testing
Authors: Linfeng Liang, Xiao Cheng, Tsong Yueh Chen, Xi Zheng
Venue: Proceedings of the ACM on Software Engineering, Vol. 3, FSE, Article FSE146, July 2026. Article FSE146 (July 2026),
First: 2026-04-20T23:49:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T23:49:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Simulation-based testing of autonomous driving systems (ADS) must uncover realistic and diverse failures in dense, heterogeneous traffic. However, existing search-based seeding methods (e.g., genetic algorithms) struggle in high-dimensional spaces, often collapsing to limited modes and missing many failure scenarios. We present PtoP, a framework that combines adaptive random seed generation with Stein Variational Gradient Descent (SVGD) to produce diverse, failure-inducing initial conditions. SVGD balances attraction toward high-risk regions and repulsion among particles, yielding risk-seeking yet well-distributed seeds across multiple failure modes. PtoP is plug-and-play and enhances existing online testing methods (e.g., reinforcement learning--based testers) by providing principled seeds. Evaluation in CARLA on two industry-grade ADS (Apollo, Autoware) and a native end-to-end system shows that PtoP improves safety violation rate (up to 27.68%), scenario diversity (9.6%), and map coverage (16.78%) over baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从粒子到风险：基于SVGD的自动驾驶系统测试危险场景生成
自动驾驶系统（ADS）的仿真测试必须在密集异构交通中发现真实且多样化的故障。然而，现有基于搜索的种子生成方法（如遗传算法）在高维空间中表现不佳，常陷入有限模式而遗漏大量故障场景。我们提出PtoP框架，结合自适应随机种子生成与Stein变分梯度下降（SVGD），以产生多样化的故障诱导初始条件。SVGD平衡了高风险区域的吸引力和粒子间的排斥力，从而生成跨多种故障模式的风险导向且分布均匀的种子。PtoP具备即插即用特性，可通过提供理论化种子增强现有在线测试方法（如基于强化学习的测试器）。在CARLA中对两款工业级ADS（Apollo、Autoware）及一个原生端到端系统的评估表明，PtoP相较于基线方法，在安全违规率（最高提升27.68%）、场景多样性（提升9.6%）和地图覆盖率（提升16.78%）方面均有改进。

Collaborative Contextual Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Chih-Yu Chang, Qiyuan Chen, Tianhan Gao, David Fenning, Chinedum Okwudire, Neil Dasgupta, Wei Lu, Raed Al Kontar
First: 2026-04-20T23:28:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T23:28:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Discovering optimal designs through sequential data collection is essential in many real-world applications. While Bayesian Optimization (BO) has achieved remarkable success in this setting, growing attention has recently turned to context-specific optimal design, formalized as Contextual Bayesian Optimization (CBO). Unlike BO, CBO is inherently more challenging as it must approximate an entire mapping from the context space to its corresponding optimal design, requiring simultaneous exploration across contexts and exploitation within each. In many modern applications, such tasks arise across multiple potentially heterogeneous but related clients, where collaboration can significantly improve learning efficiency. We propose CCBO, Collaborative Contextual Bayesian Optimization, a unified framework enabling multiple clients to jointly perform CBO with controllable contexts, supporting both online collaboration and offline initialization from peers' historical beliefs, with an optional privacy-preserving communication mechanism. We establish sublinear regret guarantees and demonstrate, through extensive simulations and a real-world hot rolling application, that CCBO achieves substantial improvements over existing approaches even under client heterogeneity. The code to reproduce the results can be found at https://github.com/cchihyu/Collaborative-Contextual-Bayesian-Optimization
中文标题/摘要
标题：协同上下文贝叶斯优化
通过序列化数据收集发现最优设计在许多实际应用中至关重要。虽然贝叶斯优化（BO）在此场景中已取得显著成功，但近期研究日益关注上下文特定的最优设计问题，即形式化为上下文贝叶斯优化（CBO）。与BO不同，CBO本质上更具挑战性，因其需近似从上下文空间到对应最优设计的完整映射，要求跨上下文的同步探索与各上下文内的深度挖掘。在许多现代应用中，此类任务出现在多个潜在异构但相关的客户端之间，协同合作可显著提升学习效率。我们提出协同上下文贝叶斯优化（CCBO）——一个支持多客户端在可控上下文环境下联合执行CBO的统一框架，兼具在线协同与基于同伴历史信念的离线初始化能力，并提供可选的隐私保护通信机制。我们建立了次线性遗憾的理论保证，并通过大量仿真与真实热轧应用验证：即使在客户端异构条件下，CCBO相较现有方法仍能实现显著性能提升。代码详见：https://github.com/cchihyu/Collaborative-Contextual-Bayesian-Optimization
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of discovering optimal designs across varying contexts, a problem formalized as Contextual Bayesian Optimization (CBO), which is more complex than standard Bayesian Optimization due to the need to map contexts to optimal designs. To improve efficiency in multi-client settings where tasks are related but potentially heterogeneous, the authors propose Collaborative Contextual Bayesian Optimization (CCBO), a framework that enables clients to collaborate online or use offline historical data from peers, with optional privacy-preserving communication. Experimental results, including simulations and a real-world hot rolling application, demonstrate that CCBO achieves sublinear regret guarantees and significantly outperforms existing methods, even under client heterogeneity.
本文针对在不同上下文中寻找最优设计的问题，即上下文贝叶斯优化（CBO），该问题比标准贝叶斯优化更复杂，因为它需要将上下文映射到最优设计。为了提高多客户端环境中任务相关但可能异质时的效率，作者提出了协作上下文贝叶斯优化（CCBO），该框架允许客户端在线协作或使用同行的离线历史数据，并可选隐私保护通信机制。实验结果表明，包括模拟和实际热轧应用，CCBO实现了次线性遗憾保证，并在客户端异质性下显著优于现有方法。
RIFT: A RubrIc Failure Mode Taxonomy and Automated Diagnostics
Authors: Zhengyang Qi, Charles Dickens, Derek Pham, Amanda Dsouza, Armin Parchami, Frederic Sala, Paroma Varma
First: 2026-04-01T20:34:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T23:25:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rubric-based evaluation is widely used in LLM benchmarks and training pipelines for open-ended, less verifiable tasks. While prior work has demonstrated the effectiveness of rubrics using downstream signals such as reinforcement learning outcomes, there remains no principled way to diagnose how a rubric itself fails from such aggregated or downstream signals alone. To address this gap, we introduce RIFT: RubrIc Failure mode Taxonomy, a taxonomy for systematically characterizing failure modes in rubric composition and design. RIFT consists of eight failure modes organized into three high-level categories: Reliability Failures, Content Validity Failures, and Consequential Validity Failures. RIFT is developed using grounded theory by iteratively annotating rubrics drawn from five diverse data sources spanning general instruction following, code generation, creative writing, and expert-level deep research, until no new failure modes are identified. We evaluate the consistency of the taxonomy by measuring agreement among independent human annotators, observing fair agreement overall (87% pairwise agreement and 0.64 average Cohen's kappa). Finally, to support scalable diagnosis, we propose automated rubric quality metrics and show that they align with human failure-mode annotations, achieving up to 0.925 F1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RIFT：一种评估准则失效模式分类体系与自动化诊断方法
基于评估准则的测评方法广泛应用于大语言模型开放式、难验证任务的基准测试与训练流程。尽管先前研究已通过强化学习结果等下游信号验证了评估准则的有效性，但仅从聚合或下游信号出发，仍缺乏系统性诊断评估准则自身失效原因的理论方法。为填补这一空白，我们提出RIFT：评估准则失效模式分类体系，该体系系统化表征评估准则构建与设计中的失效模式。RIFT包含八大失效模式，归入三个高层级类别：可靠性失效、内容效度失效与结果效度失效。本研究采用扎根理论方法，通过迭代标注来自五大跨领域数据源（涵盖通用指令遵循、代码生成、创意写作及专家级深度研究）的评估准则直至未发现新失效模式，从而构建该分类体系。通过测量独立标注者间一致性评估分类体系的稳定性，整体达到中等一致性水平（配对一致率87%，平均科恩卡帕系数0.64）。最后，为支持规模化诊断，我们提出自动化评估准则质量指标，并证明其与人工失效模式标注具有高度一致性，最高F1分数达0.925。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the lack of systematic methods to diagnose failures in rubric design for LLM evaluation, despite rubrics' widespread use. The authors introduce RIFT, a taxonomy of eight failure modes across three categories, developed via grounded theory by annotating rubrics from diverse domains. Experimental results show fair inter-annotator agreement and that automated metrics align well with human annotations, achieving up to 0.925 F1 score.
本研究旨在解决LLM评估中评分准则设计缺乏系统性故障诊断方法的问题。作者提出了RIFT分类法，通过扎根理论对多领域准则进行标注，定义了八个故障模式。实验结果表明标注者间一致性较高，且自动化指标与人工标注高度吻合，F1分数最高达0.925。
Semantic Interaction Information mediates compositional generalization in latent space
Authors: John Schwarcz
First: 2026-03-28T04:46:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T20:11:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Are there still barriers to generalization once all relevant variables are known? We address this question via a framework that casts compositional generalization as a variational inference problem over latent variables with parametric interactions. To explore this, we develop the Cognitive Gridworld, a stationary Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) where observations are generated jointly by multiple latent variables, yet feedback is provided for only a single goal variable. This setting allows us to define Semantic Interaction Information (SII): a metric measuring the contribution of latent variable interactions to task performance. Using SII, we analyze Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs) provided with these interactions, finding that SII explains the accuracy gap between Echo State and Fully Trained networks. Our analysis also uncovers a theoretically predicted failure mode where confidence decouples from accuracy, suggesting that utilizing interactions between relevant variables is a non-trivial capability. We then address a harder regime where the interactions must be learned by an embedding model. Learning how latent variables interact requires accurate inference, yet accurate inference depends on knowing those interactions. The Cognitive Gridworld reveals this circular dependence as a core challenge for continual meta-learning. We approach this dilemma via Representation Classification Chains (RCCs), a JEPA-style architecture that disentangles these processes: variable inference and variable embeddings are learned by separate modules through Reinforcement Learning and self-supervised learning, respectively. Lastly, we demonstrate that RCCs facilitate compositional generalization to novel combinations of relevant variables. Together, these results establish a grounded setting for evaluating goal-directed generalist agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语义交互信息在潜在空间中调节组合泛化
当所有相关变量已知时，泛化是否仍存在障碍？我们通过一个将组合泛化建模为含参数交互的潜在变量变分推断问题的框架来探讨此问题。为此，我们开发了认知网格世界——一个静态部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），其观测值由多个潜在变量共同生成，但反馈仅针对单一目标变量提供。该设定允许我们定义语义交互信息（SII）：一种衡量潜在变量交互对任务性能贡献的度量指标。利用SII，我们分析了具备这些交互能力的循环神经网络（RNN），发现SII能够解释回声状态网络与完全训练网络之间的精度差距。我们的分析还揭示了一种理论预测的失效模式，即置信度与精度解耦，这表明利用相关变量间的交互是一项非平凡的能力。 随后，我们研究了一个更困难的机制：交互必须通过嵌入模型学习。学习潜在变量的交互需要精确推断，而精确推断又依赖于了解这些交互。认知网格世界揭示了这种循环依赖是持续元学习的核心挑战。我们通过表示分类链（RCC）——一种JEPA风格架构——来解决这一困境，该架构将变量推断与变量嵌入学习解耦：分别通过强化学习和自监督学习由不同模块学习。最后，我们证明RCC能够促进对相关变量新组合的组合泛化。这些结果共同为评估目标导向的通用智能体建立了坚实基础。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether knowing all relevant variables is sufficient for compositional generalization, proposing a framework that treats it as a variational inference problem over latent variables with parametric interactions. To explore this, the authors introduce the Cognitive Gridworld, a stationary POMDP where observations stem from multiple latent variables but feedback targets only a goal variable, enabling the definition of Semantic Interaction Information (SII) to quantify how latent variable interactions affect task performance. Experiments with Recurrent Neural Networks show that SII explains accuracy differences between network types and reveals a failure mode where confidence detaches from accuracy, indicating that leveraging interactions is non-trivial. For harder cases where interactions must be learned, the paper presents Representation Classification Chains (RCCs), an architecture that separates variable inference and embedding learning via reinforcement and self-supervised learning, respectively, and demonstrates that RCCs enable generalization to novel variable combinations, offering a testbed for goal-directed agents.
本文探讨了在已知所有相关变量的情况下，组合泛化是否仍存在障碍，提出了一个将组合泛化视为潜在变量参数交互的变分推断问题的框架。为此，作者设计了认知网格世界，这是一个静态部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，其中观测由多个潜在变量共同生成，但反馈仅针对单个目标变量，从而定义了语义交互信息（SII）来量化潜在变量交互对任务性能的影响。对循环神经网络的实验表明，SII解释了不同类型网络间的准确率差距，并揭示了一种置信度与准确度解耦的故障模式，表明利用变量交互并非易事。针对需要学习交互的更困难场景，本文提出了表示分类链（RCCs）架构，通过强化学习和自监督学习分别分离变量推断和嵌入学习，并证明RCCs能促进对新变量组合的泛化，为评估目标导向的通用智能体提供了基础测试环境。
ARES: Adaptive Red-Teaming and End-to-End Repair of Policy-Reward System
Authors: Jiacheng Liang, Yao Ma, Tharindu Kumarage, Satyapriya Krishna, Rahul Gupta, Kai-Wei Chang, Aram Galstyan, Charith Peris
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-20T19:54:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T19:54:47+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, ACL 2026 Main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) is central to aligning Large Language Models (LLMs), yet it introduces a critical vulnerability: an imperfect Reward Model (RM) can become a single point of failure when it fails to penalize unsafe behaviors. While existing red-teaming approaches primarily target policy-level weaknesses, they overlook what we term systemic weaknesses cases where both the core LLM and the RM fail in tandem. We present ARES, a framework that systematically discovers and mitigates such dual vulnerabilities. ARES employs a ``Safety Mentor'' that dynamically composes semantically coherent adversarial prompts by combining structured component types (topics, personas, tactics, goals) and generates corresponding malicious and safe responses. This dual-targeting approach exposes weaknesses in both the core LLM and the RM simultaneously. Using the vulnerabilities gained, ARES implements a two-stage repair process: first fine-tuning the RM to better detect harmful content, then leveraging the improved RM to optimize the core model. Experiments across multiple adversarial safety benchmarks demonstrate that ARES substantially enhances safety robustness while preserving model capabilities, establishing a new paradigm for comprehensive RLHF safety alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARES：策略-奖励系统的自适应红队测试与端到端修复框架
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）是大语言模型（LLM）对齐的核心技术，但其存在一个关键脆弱性：当不完善的奖励模型（RM）未能有效惩罚不安全行为时，可能成为单点故障。现有红队测试方法主要针对策略层面的弱点，却忽视了系统级弱点——即核心LLM与RM同时失效的情况。 我们提出ARES框架，系统性地发现并缓解此类双重脆弱性。ARES采用“安全导师”模块，通过组合结构化组件类型（主题、角色、策略、目标）动态生成语义连贯的对抗性提示，并同步生成对应的恶意与安全响应。这种双重目标攻击能同时暴露核心LLM与RM的弱点。基于发现的脆弱性，ARES实施两阶段修复流程：首先微调RM以提升有害内容检测能力，再利用优化后的RM改进核心模型。在多个对抗性安全基准测试中，ARES在保持模型能力的同时显著增强了安全鲁棒性，为全面RLHF安全对齐建立了新范式。

The paper addresses a critical vulnerability in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) where an imperfect Reward Model (RM) can fail to penalize unsafe behaviors, creating systemic weaknesses when both the core LLM and RM fail together. To tackle this, the authors propose ARES, a framework that uses a Safety Mentor to dynamically generate semantically coherent adversarial prompts targeting both the LLM and RM, thereby exposing dual vulnerabilities. Experimental results across multiple safety benchmarks show that ARES significantly improves safety robustness while maintaining model capabilities, offering a comprehensive approach to RLHF alignment.

When and What to Ask: AskBench and Rubric-Guided RLVR for LLM Clarification
Authors: Jiale Zhao, Ke Fang, Lu Cheng
First: 2026-02-04T02:21:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T19:24:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) often respond even when prompts omit critical details or include misleading information, leading to hallucinations or reinforced misconceptions. We study how to evaluate and improve LLMs' ability to decide when and what to ask for clarification without sacrificing task performance. We introduce AskBench, an interactive benchmark that converts standard QA pairs into multi-turn interactions with explicit checkpoints. A unified judge loop evaluates final answers and simulates user responses as needed. AskBench covers two settings: AskMind, with intent-deficient queries requiring clarification, and AskOverconfidence, with queries containing false premises that must be identified and corrected. We further propose rubric-guided reinforcement learning with verifier-based rewards (RLVR), which uses structured rubrics to encourage targeted clarification. Experiments show consistent improvements in accuracy, rubric adherence, and interaction efficiency, with strong generalization to unseen domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：何时提问与提问内容：AskBench与基于量规的RLVR用于大语言模型澄清机制
大语言模型常在提示缺失关键细节或包含误导信息时仍作出回应，导致幻觉或强化错误认知。本研究探讨如何在不影响任务性能的前提下，评估并提升大语言模型决定何时及如何请求澄清的能力。我们提出AskBench交互式基准，将标准问答对转化为含明确检查点的多轮交互，通过统一评判循环评估最终答案并模拟用户响应。AskBench涵盖两种场景：AskMind（需澄清意图缺失的查询）和AskOverconfidence（需识别并修正含错误前提的查询）。进一步提出基于量规的强化学习与验证器奖励机制，利用结构化量规引导针对性澄清。实验表明该方法在准确性、量规遵循度和交互效率上持续提升，并对未见领域展现出强泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The study addresses the problem of large language models (LLMs) generating responses to ambiguous or misleading prompts, which can lead to hallucinations. To evaluate and enhance LLMs' ability to seek clarification appropriately, the authors introduce AskBench, an interactive benchmark that transforms standard question-answer pairs into multi-turn dialogues with checkpoints, covering both intent-deficient queries (AskMind) and queries with false premises (AskOverconfidence). They also propose rubric-guided reinforcement learning with verifier-based rewards (RLVR) to encourage structured clarification. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach improves accuracy, adherence to clarification rubrics, and interaction efficiency, with good generalization to new domains.

ExpertGen: Scalable Sim-to-Real Expert Policy Learning from Imperfect Behavior Priors
Authors: Zifan Xu, Ran Gong, Maria Vittoria Minniti, Ahmet Salih Gundogdu, Eric Rosen, Kausik Sivakumar, Riedana Yan, Zixing Wang, Di Deng, Peter Stone, Xiaohan Zhang, Karl Schmeckpeper
First: 2026-03-16T22:12:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T19:05:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning generalizable and robust behavior cloning policies requires large volumes of high-quality robotics data. While human demonstrations (e.g., through teleoperation) serve as the standard source for expert behaviors, acquiring such data at scale in the real world is prohibitively expensive. This paper introduces ExpertGen, a framework that automates expert policy learning in simulation to enable scalable sim-to-real transfer. ExpertGen first initializes a behavior prior using a diffusion policy trained on imperfect demonstrations, which may be synthesized by large language models or provided by humans. Reinforcement learning is then used to steer this prior toward high task success by optimizing the diffusion model's initial noise while keep original policy frozen. By keeping the pretrained diffusion policy frozen, ExpertGen regularizes exploration to remain within safe, human-like behavior manifolds, while also enabling effective learning with only sparse rewards. Empirical evaluations on challenging manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that ExpertGen reliably produces high-quality expert policies with no reward engineering. On industrial assembly tasks, ExpertGen achieves a 90.5% overall success rate, while on long-horizon manipulation tasks it attains 85% overall success, outperforming all baseline methods. The resulting policies exhibit dexterous control and remain robust across diverse initial configurations and failure states. To validate sim-to-real transfer, the learned state-based expert policies are further distilled into visuomotor policies via DAgger and successfully deployed on real robotic hardware.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ExpertGen：基于不完美行为先验的可扩展仿真到现实专家策略学习
学习泛化性强且鲁棒的行为克隆策略需要大量高质量的机器人数据。虽然人类演示（如通过遥操作）是专家行为的标准来源，但在现实世界中大规模获取此类数据成本极高。本文提出ExpertGen框架，通过在仿真环境中自动化专家策略学习，实现可扩展的仿真到现实迁移。ExpertGen首先利用在不完美演示数据上训练的扩散策略初始化行为先验，这些演示可由大语言模型合成或由人类提供。随后通过强化学习优化扩散模型的初始噪声（同时保持原始策略冻结），引导该先验实现高任务成功率。通过冻结预训练的扩散策略，ExpertGen将探索范围正则化至安全、类人的行为流形内，同时仅需稀疏奖励即可实现高效学习。在具有挑战性的操作基准测试中，实证评估表明ExpertGen无需奖励工程即可稳定生成高质量专家策略。在工业装配任务中达到90.5%的总成功率，在长时程操作任务中达到85%的总成功率，均优于所有基线方法。所得策略展现出灵巧的控制能力，并在多样化初始配置与故障状态下保持鲁棒性。为验证仿真到现实迁移，学习到的基于状态的专家策略通过DAgger进一步蒸馏为视觉运动策略，并成功部署于真实机器人硬件。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for ExpertGen arises from the high cost and difficulty of acquiring large-scale, high-quality human demonstrations for robotics, which are needed for robust behavior cloning. The method introduces a framework that automates expert policy learning in simulation for scalable sim-to-real transfer by first initializing a behavior prior with a diffusion policy trained on imperfect demonstrations, then using reinforcement learning to steer this prior toward high task success by optimizing the initial noise while keeping the original policy frozen to regularize exploration. Experimental results on manipulation benchmarks show that ExpertGen reliably produces high-quality policies without reward engineering, achieving a 90.5% overall success rate on industrial assembly tasks and 85% on long-horizon manipulation tasks, outperforming baselines, with the policies demonstrating dexterous control and robustness, and successful sim-to-real transfer via distillation into visuomotor policies.
ExpertGen的动机源于获取大规模高质量机器人演示数据的高成本和困难，这些数据对于鲁棒的行为克隆至关重要。该方法提出了一个框架，通过在仿真中自动化专家策略学习来实现可扩展的仿真到现实迁移，首先使用基于不完美演示训练的扩散策略初始化行为先验，然后通过强化学习优化初始噪声来引导该先验实现高任务成功率，同时保持原始策略冻结以规范探索。在操作基准测试中的实验结果表明，ExpertGen无需奖励工程即可可靠地生成高质量策略，在工业装配任务中达到90.5%的总成功率，在长时程操作任务中达到85%，优于所有基线方法，且策略展现出灵巧控制和鲁棒性，并通过蒸馏为视觉运动策略成功实现了仿真到现实的迁移。
Discrete Tilt Matching
Authors: Yuyuan Chen, Shiyi Wang, Peter Potaptchik, Jaeyeon Kim, Michael S. Albergo
First: 2026-04-20T18:43:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T18:43:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Masked diffusion large language models (dLLMs) are a promising alternative to autoregressive generation. While reinforcement learning (RL) methods have recently been adapted to dLLM fine-tuning, their objectives typically depend on sequence-level marginal likelihoods, which are intractable for masked diffusion models. To address this, we derive Discrete Tilt Matching (DTM), a likelihood-free method that recasts dLLM fine-tuning as state-level matching of local unmasking posteriors under reward tilting. DTM takes the form of a weighted cross-entropy objective with explicit minimizer, and admits control variates that improve training stability. On a synthetic maze-planning task, we analyze how DTM's annealing schedule and control variates affect training stability and prevent mode collapse. At scale, fine-tuning LLaDA-8B-Instruct with DTM yields strong gains on Sudoku and Countdown while remaining competitive on MATH500 and GSM8K.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离散倾斜匹配
掩码扩散大语言模型（dLLMs）是自回归生成的一种有前景的替代方案。虽然强化学习（RL）方法最近已应用于dLLM微调，但其目标通常依赖于序列级边际似然，这对于掩码扩散模型是难以处理的。为此，我们提出了离散倾斜匹配（DTM），这是一种无需似然的方法，将dLLM微调重新定义为奖励倾斜下局部去掩码后验的状态级匹配。DTM采用带显式最小化器的加权交叉熵目标形式，并引入可提升训练稳定性的控制变量。在合成迷宫规划任务中，我们分析了DTM的退火策略和控制变量如何影响训练稳定性并防止模式崩溃。在大规模实验中，使用DTM微调LLaDA-8B-Instruct模型在数独和倒计时任务上取得显著提升，同时在MATH500和GSM8K基准上保持竞争力。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces Discrete Tilt Matching (DTM), a method for fine-tuning masked diffusion large language models (dLLMs) to align with reward signals, addressing the intractability of sequence-level marginal likelihoods in such models. The approach reformulates fine-tuning as matching state-level local unmasking posteriors under a reward-tilted distribution, resulting in a weighted cross-entropy objective with an explicit minimizer and incorporating control variates to enhance stability. Experimental results demonstrate DTM's effectiveness in preventing mode collapse on a synthetic maze-planning task and show that fine-tuning LLaDA-8B-Instruct with DTM yields significant improvements on Sudoku and Countdown tasks while maintaining competitive performance on MATH500 and GSM8K.

Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yunke Ao, Le Chen, Bruce D. Lee, Assefa S. Wahd, Aline Czarnobai, Philipp Fürnstahl, Bernhard Schölkopf, Andreas Krause
First: 2026-04-20T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:59:01+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) has become the predominant algorithm for on-policy reinforcement learning due to its scalability and empirical robustness across domains. However, there is a significant disconnect between the underlying foundations of trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective used in PPO. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework. We formulate a novel regularized and constrained policy optimization problem and derive its analytical optimal solution. We prove that this solution ensures monotonic performance improvement. To handle parameterized policy classes, we develop a policy optimization algorithm called Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) that minimizes an advantage-weighted divergence between the policy and the analytic optimal solution from BRRL. We further establish a lower bound on the expected performance of the resulting policy in terms of the BPO loss function. Notably, our framework also provides a new theoretical lens to interpret the success of the PPO loss, and connects trust region policy optimization and the Cross-Entropy Method (CEM). We additionally extend BPO to Group-relative BPO (GBPO) for LLM fine-tuning. Empirical evaluations of BPO across MuJoCo, Atari, and complex IsaacLab environments (e.g., Humanoid locomotion), and of GBPO for LLM fine-tuning tasks, demonstrate that BPO and GBPO generally match or outperform PPO and GRPO in stability and final performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有界比率强化学习
近端策略优化（PPO）因其可扩展性和跨领域的经验鲁棒性，已成为同策略强化学习的主导算法。然而，信任域方法的基础理论与PPO中使用的启发式截断目标之间存在显著脱节。本文通过引入有界比率强化学习（BRRL）框架来弥合这一差距。我们构建了一个新颖的正则化约束策略优化问题，并推导出其解析最优解。我们证明该解能确保性能的单调改进。为处理参数化策略类，我们开发了一种名为有界策略优化（BPO）的策略优化算法，该算法最小化策略与BRRL解析最优解之间的优势加权散度。我们进一步基于BPO损失函数建立了所得策略期望性能的下界。值得注意的是，本框架还为解释PPO损失的成功提供了新的理论视角，并连接了信任域策略优化与交叉熵方法（CEM）。我们还将BPO扩展至适用于大语言模型微调的组相对BPO（GBPO）。在MuJoCo、Atari和复杂IsaacLab环境（如人形机器人运动）中对BPO的实证评估，以及在大语言模型微调任务中对GBPO的评估表明，BPO和GBPO在稳定性和最终性能上通常匹配或优于PPO和GRPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the disconnect between the theoretical foundations of trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective used in Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) by introducing the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework. The method formulates a regularized and constrained policy optimization problem, derives its analytical optimal solution which guarantees monotonic improvement, and develops the Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) algorithm to minimize an advantage-weighted divergence between the policy and this optimal solution. Experimental results across MuJoCo, Atari, and IsaacLab environments show that BPO matches or outperforms PPO in stability and final performance, and its extension, Group-relative BPO (GBPO), also demonstrates effectiveness for LLM fine-tuning tasks.
本文针对近端策略优化（PPO）中信任域方法理论基础与启发式裁剪目标之间的脱节问题，提出了有界比率强化学习（BRRL）框架。该方法构建了一个正则化约束的策略优化问题，推导出其保证性能单调提升的解析最优解，并开发了有界策略优化（BPO）算法，以最小化策略与该最优解之间的优势加权散度。在MuJoCo、Atari和IsaacLab等环境中的实验结果表明，BPO在稳定性和最终性能上匹配或优于PPO，其扩展方法——组相对BPO（GBPO）在大语言模型微调任务中也表现出有效性。
When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision?
Authors: Salman Rahman, Jingyan Shen, Anna Mordvina, Hamid Palangi, Saadia Gabriel, Pavel Izmailov
First: 2026-04-20T17:57:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:57:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models have achieved significant reasoning improvements through reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). Yet as model capabilities grow, constructing high-quality reward signals becomes increasingly difficult, making it essential to understand when RLVR can succeed under weaker forms of supervision. We conduct a systematic empirical study across diverse model families and reasoning domains under three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. We find that generalization is governed by training reward saturation dynamics: models that generalize exhibit a prolonged pre-saturation phase during which training reward and downstream performance climb together, while models that saturate rapidly memorize rather than learn. We identify reasoning faithfulness, defined as the extent to which intermediate steps logically support the final answer, as the pre-RL property that predicts which regime a model falls into, while output diversity alone is uninformative. Motivated by these findings, we disentangle the contributions of continual pre-training and supervised fine-tuning, finding that SFT on explicit reasoning traces is necessary for generalization under weak supervision, while continual pre-training on domain data amplifies the effect. Applied together to Llama3.2-3B-Base, these interventions enable generalization across all three settings where the base model previously failed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型何时能在弱监督下学会推理？
大语言模型通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在推理能力上取得了显著提升。然而，随着模型能力的增强，构建高质量奖励信号变得日益困难，因此理解RLVR在何种弱监督条件下能够成功至关重要。我们在三种弱监督设置（数据稀缺、奖励噪声、自监督代理奖励）下，对不同模型系列和推理领域进行了系统性实证研究。研究发现，泛化能力受训练奖励饱和动态的支配：能够泛化的模型在训练中会经历较长的预饱和阶段，此阶段训练奖励与下游性能同步提升；而快速饱和的模型则倾向于记忆而非学习。我们将推理忠实性（定义为中间步骤对最终答案的逻辑支持程度）确定为预测模型所属机制的关键预强化学习属性，而仅凭输出多样性则无法提供有效信息。基于这些发现，我们分离了持续预训练与监督微调的贡献：发现对显式推理轨迹进行监督微调是弱监督下实现泛化的必要条件，而对领域数据的持续预训练则会放大这一效果。将这些干预措施共同应用于Llama3.2-3B-Base模型后，使其在基础模型先前失败的三种设置中均实现了泛化。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates when large language models can learn reasoning under weak supervision, motivated by the difficulty of obtaining high-quality reward signals as models scale. The authors conduct an empirical study across model families and reasoning domains using three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. They find that generalization depends on training reward saturation dynamics, where models that generalize show a prolonged pre-saturation phase with correlated improvements in training reward and downstream performance, while rapid saturation leads to memorization. Reasoning faithfulness, the logical support of intermediate steps for the final answer, is identified as a key pre-reinforcement learning predictor, whereas output diversity is not informative. The study further shows that supervised fine-tuning on explicit reasoning traces is essential for generalization under weak supervision, and continual pre-training on domain data enhances this effect, as demonstrated by enabling generalization in Llama3.2-3B-Base across all three settings where it previously failed.
本文研究大型语言模型在弱监督下何时能学会推理，其动机在于随着模型规模扩大，获取高质量奖励信号变得日益困难。作者通过在不同模型系列和推理领域进行实证研究，探索了三种弱监督设置：稀缺数据、噪声奖励和自监督代理奖励。研究发现泛化能力取决于训练奖励饱和动态，泛化良好的模型表现出延长的预饱和阶段，其中训练奖励与下游性能同步提升，而快速饱和则导致记忆而非学习。推理忠实性，即中间步骤对最终答案的逻辑支持程度，被确定为预测模型所处机制的关键预强化学习属性，而输出多样性则无信息量。研究进一步表明，在弱监督下，对显式推理轨迹进行监督微调是泛化所必需的，而领域数据的持续预训练能放大此效果，这在Llama3.2-3B-Base模型中得到验证，使其在先前失败的三种设置中均实现了泛化。
Empowering Multi-Turn Tool-Integrated Agentic Reasoning with Group Turn Policy Optimization
Authors: Yifeng Ding, Hung Le, Songyang Han, Kangrui Ruan, Zhenghui Jin, Varun Kumar, Zijian Wang, Anoop Deoras
First: 2025-11-18T19:01:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:40:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training Large Language Models (LLMs) for multi-turn Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) - where models iteratively reason, generate code, and verify through execution - remains challenging for existing reinforcement learning (RL) approaches. Current RL methods, exemplified by Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), suffer from coarse-grained, trajectory-level rewards that provide insufficient learning signals for complex multi-turn interactions, leading to training stagnation. To address this issue, we propose Group Turn Policy Optimization (GTPO), a novel RL algorithm specifically designed for training LLMs on multi-turn TIR tasks. GTPO introduces three key innovations: (1) turn-level reward assignment that provides fine-grained feedback for individual turns, (2) return-based advantage estimation where normalized discounted returns are calculated as advantages, and (3) self-supervised reward shaping that exploits self-supervision signals from generated code to densify sparse binary outcome-based rewards. Our comprehensive evaluation demonstrates that GTPO outperforms GRPO by 3.0% across diverse math reasoning benchmarks, establishing its effectiveness. GTPO also improves GRPO by 3.9% on commonsense reasoning and program synthesis tasks, demonstrating its generalizability to non-math domains. Importantly, GTPO incurs negligible overhead, ensuring its practicality for real-world scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于组轮次策略优化的多轮工具集成智能体推理能力增强
针对多轮工具集成推理任务训练大语言模型——即模型通过迭代推理、生成代码并执行验证的过程——现有强化学习方法仍面临挑战。以组相对策略优化为代表的当前RL方法存在奖励信号粒度粗糙、仅提供轨迹级反馈的问题，难以支撑复杂多轮交互的学习需求，易导致训练停滞。为此，我们提出专为多轮TIR任务设计的强化学习新算法——组轮次策略优化。该算法包含三项核心创新：(1) 提供细粒度反馈的轮次级奖励分配机制，(2) 以归一化折现回报计算优势值的回报基准优势估计方法，(3) 利用生成代码自监督信号对稀疏二元结果奖励进行稠密化重塑的自监督奖励塑形技术。综合评估表明，GTPO在多样化数学推理基准上超越GRPO达3.0%，在常识推理与程序合成任务上提升3.9%，验证了其跨领域泛化能力。该算法仅产生可忽略的开销，具备实际部署的可行性。

To overcome this, the authors propose Group Turn Policy Optimization (GTPO), which introduces turn-level reward assignment, return-based advantage estimation, and self-supervised reward shaping to provide fine-grained feedback. Experimental results show GTPO outperforms GRPO by 3.0% on math reasoning benchmarks and by 3.9% on commonsense reasoning and program synthesis tasks, demonstrating effectiveness and generalizability with negligible overhead.
